According to Mo's speech criticizing Fascism today, it has been the second time in two days. Yesterday, Mo also had a speech criticizing Fascism at the All-Union Congress as follows: "We do not need alliances or协的, what we rely on is our own growing strength. We are very busy dealing with our own domestic affairs, and we have no time to pay attention to foreign conspiracies. However, for the sake of peace, we are willing to cooperate with other countries within the framework of the League of Nations. Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations is for the freedom of aggression. The German-Japanese agreement is nothing more than a smokescreen for an anti-Soviet war. At present, there are two forces in the world, namely communism that tends to peace and fascism that tends to war." (Reuters dispatch, 30th)

(Moscow) Air Force Deputy Commander Kipulin claimed in a speech at the All-Union Congress here today that next year, the Soviet Air Force will be the first in the world in terms of quality and quantity. This year, the Soviet Air Force that can fight will have 100,000 people, and the national aircraft production last year has doubled. Kipushi continued, "At present, we have hundreds of air force fighters with a speed of 360 miles per hour, which can parachute a battalion of fully armed soldiers behind the enemy in ten minutes." Kipushi finally said, "If Germany invades the Soviet Union, it will not be spared from disaster." (Reuters dispatch, 29th)

(Moscow) Soviet Air Force Deputy Commander Kliben reported to the Soviet National Congress today that the Soviet Union has 7,000 fighter planes, more than any country in the world. Germany has between 6,000 and 7,000 fighter planes. The Soviet Union and Germany each have 1,000 first-line aircraft, but in terms of combat effectiveness, the Soviet Air Force is the best in the world. Keli's report surprised foreign observers, because according to foreign estimates, the total number of Soviet aircraft is less than 4,000. Keli continued, according to the figures released by Germany, Japan has 2,500 aircraft, the United States 2,700, and France 2,200. At present, Germany, Italy, and Japan need aircraft more urgently than any country, so the arms race is in progress. At present, there are 17,000 to 18,000 aircraft in various capitalist countries, which will be increased to 17,000 to 18,000 in the next two years. In the past ten months, the Soviet Union has manufactured 94.5% more aircraft than the total output last year. The number of army aircraft is now four times more than in 1932. Most of them can reach a speed of 315 miles per hour, and can be increased to 420 miles per hour. If Germany has 75,000 drivers in the near future, the Soviet Union will have 100,000. If the German National Socialists dare to threaten the Soviet Union with the Air Force, they will definitely be unfortunate. In addition, it is known that the Soviet Union also has many three-engine bombers that can carry heavy loads, but their speed is slower than that of British, German, and American bombers. Soviet factories are now trying their best to manufacture high-speed aircraft. (29th, Kuomintang dispatch)

The German-Japanese Pact Does Not Contain Secret Clauses. Italy and Japan Mutually Recognize Established Facts, Which Will Be Issued by Means of Exchanging Documents. 60

(London) The British government received a telegram from Berlin today guaranteeing that there are no secret clauses in the German-Japanese Anti-Comintern Pact signed recently. Informed sources believe that this guarantee from Berlin can dispel the panic among British people that there are other unpublished clauses in the pact. (Reuters, 30th)

(Tokyo) The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs has received a telegram from Japanese Ambassador to Italy, Sugimura Yōtarō, regarding the Japanese-Italian agreement issue on the 30th. Foreign Minister Arita immediately met with Director-General of the European and Asian Affairs Bureau, Higashi Kyō, and Director-General of the Commerce Bureau, Matsushima, on the morning of the 30th to discuss the content of the instruction. The instruction will be issued by the evening of the 30th, and all the facts may be announced as soon as possible. It is said that the exchange of recognition of "Manchukuo" and the annexation of Abyssinia will be issued by means of exchanging documents, so as to avoid creating the impression of a formal agreement. In addition, a trade agreement seems to be signed. A spokesman for the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs announced today that Italy and Japan have not yet reached complete agreement, and that it is not yet time to confirm or deny the news about the recognition of "Manchukuo" and Abyssinia. When talking about the Chinese authorities' statement on the German-Japanese Anti-Comintern Pact, the spokesman said that this statement does not affect the Sino-Japanese negotiations, because Japan was fully aware of the Chinese government's attitude towards the anti-communist issue before the announcement of the German-Japanese Anti-Comintern Pact. When asked whether there is a possibility of reaching a compromise between China and Japan if the anti-communist issue is not discussed, the answer was that this is a secret and the most secret part of the Sino-Japanese negotiations. (Central News Agency dispatch, 30th)

(Rome) Regarding Italy's de facto recognition of "Manchukuo" and Japan's de facto recognition of the Italian Empire, after responsible officials here revealed the news last Saturday, informed sources recently announced that the Italian and Japanese governments have decided to issue communiqués separately today and in the middle of next week. The communiqué has been drafted after exchanging views between the Prime Minister's Office and the Japanese Embassy. What should be released today is the announcement that Japan has established a consulate general in Addis Ababa, and what should be released next week is the announcement that Italy has established a consulate general in Changchun, the capital of "Manchukuo". Regarding this level, political people believe that this method can avoid the objections of the United Kingdom and the United States, and can also satisfy the pragmatic tendencies of the Italian and Japanese diplomatic authorities, regardless of how the legal essence is. As for the reason why the two sides issued communiqués separately, it was to prevent the outside world from interpreting them as exchange conditions. In addition, since Japan's interests in East Africa are very important, the agreement reached between Japan and Italy this time is also commercially important. (Havas dispatch, 30th)

(Rome) It was officially announced here today that Chile has recognized Italy's annexation of Abyssinia. (Kuomintang, 13th)

Italian Students in Japan Arrive in Tokyo 61

(Tokyo) Two Italian students in Japan dispatched by Italy under the Japanese-Italian exchange student agreement, Eric Pibia and Stracamicioli, arrived in Tokyo on the evening of the 29th. Pibia wants to study medicine and biology, and Sioli wants to study Buddhism, for a period of three years. (Domei dispatch, 30th)

After the Establishment of the German-Japanese Pact, Japanese Prime Minister Hirota Considers New Diplomatic Policies, Pays Attention to the Reactions of Related Countries, and Sino-Japanese Negotiations Are Expected to Resume Within the Year. Japan's Attitude Towards Russia on the Fisheries Issue is Tough. 62

(Tokyo) Prime Minister Hirota has overcome the difficulties in preparing next year's budget and has signed the German-Japanese Anti-Comintern Pact. He is preparing to deal with the next session of the Diet and implement unresolved policies. It is reported that the policies of Prime Minister's considered foreign policy plan are as follows:

In the future, foreign national policies should pay attention to the impact of the Japanese-German Pact on countries with direct interests such as China, Russia, Britain, and the United States, and strive to explain the new spirit of the Pact to various countries. In particular, since there is a fisheries treaty between Japan and Russia to be signed, the best efforts should be made to eliminate Soviet suspicion, with a view to signing a fisheries treaty within the year. Sino-Japanese negotiations have been temporarily suspended due to the war in Suiyuan, but negotiations are expected to resume before the end of the year. (Domei dispatch, 30th)

(Tokyo) The Soviet-Japanese fisheries treaty, which was scheduled to be signed on the 20th, was suddenly postponed due to the Soviet Union's excuse that domestic procedures had not been completed, resulting in a standstill at present. The agricultural and forestry authorities supervising the Northern Ocean fisheries believe that the Soviet Union's disregard for international credibility and the trampling of Japan's Northern Ocean rights acquired under the Treaty of Portsmouth is unfounded, but the Soviet Union still refuses to negotiate. Therefore, the attitude of the agricultural and forestry authorities is very tough. If it is not signed by the end of this month when the treaty expires, decisive measures will be taken to maintain vested rights. If, unfortunately, the fishing season next year comes in a state without a treaty, a policy of decisively allowing those involved to fish freely has already been established. The opinions of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Navy, and the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry have also been aligned. Therefore, if it is not signed, free fishing has already been decided. Therefore, the future measures of the Soviet Union are quite noteworthy. (Domei dispatch, 30th)

League of Nations Executive Council to Convene Special Meeting to Discuss the Spanish Situation; Meeting Date Pending Decision 65

(London) The League of Nations Executive Council has convened a special meeting at the request of the Spanish government. The date will be determined after replies from all member states of the council are received tomorrow. This action by Spain is based on Article 11, Section 2 of the League of Nations covenant, which states: "Any circumstance whatever affecting international relations which threatens to disturb international peace or the good understanding between nations upon which peace depends can be brought to the attention of the Assembly or of the Council by any Member of the League." As for the two proposed meeting dates of December 7th and 14th suggested by the League Secretariat, the majority favors the 7th. However, the Chilean government has expressed its support for convening the meeting on the 14th. It is heard that, excluding opinions from countries like the Swiss Confederation and Chile, most council members believe that discussing the Spanish situation now might not be effective. In the Spanish government's request to the League of Nations Executive Council for a special meeting, it strongly criticized Italy and Germany for supporting the rebel forces and interfering in the country's civil war, stating that their actions violate international law. The recent recognition of the Nationalist government is, in effect, an act of aggression against the Spanish government. (Reuters, 30th)

(Rome) League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol's proposal to convene a League of Nations Executive Council meeting to discuss the overall situation in Spain raises the possibility of Italy withdrawing from the League. According to non-official observers here, if this happens, it will trigger a serious and dangerous situation for Italy. People here believe that the Italian and German governments' recognition of General Franco's government in Spain is entirely within their rights. If the League of Nations conference accuses Italy, Italy will not tolerate it. (Reuters, 29th)

(Rome) It is now reported that the government has decided that Italy should continue to be a member of the League of Nations, but with one limitation: if the country is criticized again in Geneva, it will immediately withdraw from the League without hesitation. (Havas, 29th)

(London) Regarding the Spanish government's request to convene the League of Nations Executive Council, Italians here recently declared that since the Valencia government is not the officially recognized government by Italy, if the League of Nations Executive Council discusses the complaints raised by such a government, Italy will refuse to send representatives to attend. However, Italy has no intention of withdrawing from the League of Nations. Italian Ambassador Grandi has never warned the British Foreign Office that discussing the Spanish civil war issue in the League of Nations would cause the most serious consequences; he has only criticized the act of convening the Executive Council. Furthermore, since the Non-Intervention Committee for the Spanish civil war is currently discussing the non-intervention issue and there is no risk of causing danger, convening the Executive Council at this time is not only useless but also harmful. (Havas, 30th)

(Geneva) It was learned today that the League of Nations Executive Council will likely meet on December 7th, at which time the Spanish government will request the League to intervene in the country's civil war. However, depending on the opinions of Britain and France, the League seems likely to reject the Spanish government's request, as Britain believes that this civil war is purely an internal affair. France also argues that the League should not investigate and should not intervene. The Non-Intervention Committee already has powers equivalent to the League of Nations to prevent other countries from openly assisting either side. Currently, it seems that only the Soviet Union supports a League of Nations investigation, while Germany and Italy naturally oppose it. (National Telegram, 29th)

Italian Soldiers Rampant in Tangier Port, Supporting Spanish Rebels Extensively 66

(London) The Liberal Party's official newspaper, the "News Chronicle," recently published a dispatch from a correspondent in Tangier, the international neutral port in North Africa, stating that Italian nationals in the port are becoming increasingly arrogant. Italian officials are doing everything they can to support the Spanish Nationalist forces. Even sailors from Italian warships docked in the port frequently come ashore, parade through the streets, and loudly sing Fascist songs, displaying great arrogance. The local Spanish and French communities view this with disapproval. The correspondent also stated that General Franco, the commander-in-chief of the Nationalist forces, had previously promised the natives of Spanish Morocco autonomous rights in exchange for their involvement in the civil war within Morocco.

Supported by Aircraft and Artillery, Spanish Rebels Launch General Offensive; Fierce Fighting Occurs in the Suburbs of Madrid; Government Launches Rocket Propaganda for the First Time 67

Talavera (Special Dispatch from Our Correspondent) This morning, the Nationalist forces launched a general offensive against the city of Madrid, covered by artillery and aircraft. The most intense attacks occurred in the northwest and south. Twenty-seven Nationalist aircraft flew over Madrid, bombing the city from low altitude. Currently, the fighting is extremely fierce in the area around the Rosales Avenue and the "De Tettuan" Barracks (southwest suburbs of Madrid). The outcome is still unknown. (Havas, 29th)

Madrid The weather in Madrid cleared up this morning, and residents feared that the Nationalist forces would resume heavy shelling. However, the government air force took the initiative, slightly reassuring the people. The government air force initially circled over the city before heading directly towards the enemy lines. Attacks by Moorish cavalry in the northwest district and near University City this morning were repelled by militiamen. The militiamen claim that the Nationalist forces suffered heavy casualties. Exciting news also arrived from other government army fronts. Government forces also launched offensives at several locations, greatly threatening the flanks of the Nationalist forces. Today, the government forces used "rocket propaganda" for the first time. These rockets were invented by a clever fireworks manufacturer in Valencia and are used to fire into Nationalist outposts. Upon landing and exploding, they release leaflets written in Spanish and Arabic, specifically targeted at foreign mercenary soldiers and Moorish soldiers, detailing the crimes and ambitions of Nationalist generals. (Reuters, 29th) The situation of unrest among the natives in Morocco is becoming increasingly serious. (Havas, 30th)

Valencia Today, the Spanish government issued a statement saying that the Nationalist forces' claim of victory west of the capital is false. The militiamen are counterattacking in that area and have advanced several miles. Government forces have also won battles in the province of Sanahuja, occupying several villages. It is reported that the enemy forces suffered heavy casualties. (Reuters, 30th)

Madrid The National Defense Council announced at noon today that rebel forces, using tank formations as cover, launched a fierce attack on the village of Pozuelo, west of Madrid. Government troops stood up to resist and engaged in hand-to-hand combat, eventually repelling the attack. The rebel forces suffered significant losses. On other fronts, artillery units from both sides continue to exchange fire. (Havas, 30th)

Talavera A government army detachment is now threatening the right flank and transportation lines of the rebel forces. As a result, the rebel forces besieging Madrid have shifted their main attack from the east of the capital to the west. Yesterday, rebel forces were very active west of the capital, occupying the village of Boadilla, eight miles from Madrid, and then advancing four miles from there towards Majadahonda. Government forces have retreated north to Alarcón. It is reported that, in addition to two hundred captured, there were four hundred casualties. The rebels are apparently attempting to cut off the Escorial highway and threaten the government army's communication lines in the Guadarrama Mountains. (Reuters, 30th)

Talavera (Special Dispatch from Our Correspondent) Yesterday morning, the Nationalist forces continued to fight in the northwest of Madrid, advancing four kilometers towards the village of Majadahonda (twelve kilometers northwest of Madrid). They also occupied the Villa Vistillas Sanatorium. In the afternoon, they continued their offensive and occupied several more high grounds, enabling them to control the village of Húmera. From then on, government forces in the Casa de Campo park area can be cleared out, thereby cutting off Madrid's communication with the city of El Escorial to the northwest, and the Nationalist forces can completely besiege the city of Madrid. (Havas, 30th)

British Parliamentary Delegation Inspects Battlefield; Narrowly Avoids Being Hit by Shells; Food Shortage in Madrid is Alarming 68

(London) British Member of Parliament Captain McNamee, a Conservative, informed a Reuters reporter via long-distance telephone last night that he and three other British MPs were nearly hit by shells while inspecting the front line, and he was fortunate to survive. While he was on the phone, the sound of artillery fire in the air was deafening. McNamee said that the food situation in the capital is appalling. Meat is unavailable, and the only dishes served in hotels are vegetables and grains. Residents waiting to buy cauliflower often have to wait for ten hours before they can get it, and it costs as much as four shillings. The platforms of underground stations are filled with refugees, and the outbreak of epidemics is likely to be very serious. One-third of the city has been reduced to rubble. (Reuters, 30th)

Thousands of Residents in the Capital City are Tragically Executed by Firing Squad, More Than Those Killed by Shellfire 69

Gibraltar A British journalist, who arrived in Gibraltar today from Madrid, stated that since the beginning of the war, approximately several thousand people in Madrid have been executed by firing squad. Most of them were executed without trial by the defending forces, and their number is actually more than those killed by Nationalist artillery. Food in the city is extremely scarce, and refugees only want one meal of rations per day. He also said that the government's reports on the Nationalist shelling of the capital are often exaggerated. Shells often land near military targets, and the Nationalist forces apparently do not want to destroy the entire city. However, since government forces have stationed themselves in churches and schools, the Nationalist forces have had to shell them. The high-rise building where the telephone company is located is the most prominent artillery target in Madrid, but the Nationalist forces have not yet fired a single shell at it. (Reuters, 30th)

Two Foreign Consuls Executed for Espionage 70

Lisbon The rebel radio station of Salamanca reported today that the Bilbao government forces executed the Austrian and Paraguayan consuls for espionage. (National Telegram, 29th)

Militiamen's Morale is High; Military Equipment is More Abundant Than Before 71

Madrid Our correspondent visited the surrounding areas of the capital to inspect the battle situation and learned that the morale of the government forces is still very high. Today's fighting was most intense in the area behind the Casa de Campo park in the northwest suburbs. Nationalist forces attempted to break through the government forces' lines using tanks as cover, but they were defeated after the government forces put up a valiant resistance. (Havas, 29th)

(London) The government forces' offensives in Oviedo and Talavera, south of Madrid, show that the government forces' strength has greatly improved. It can also indicate that the government forces have obtained a lot of foreign-supplied military equipment. A very well-informed source said that if the countries supplying the government forces were revealed to the world, everyone would be surprised. Moreover, the tactics of this counter-offensive are much more carefully planned than before, with the aim of reducing the enemy's pressure on the capital. A neutral observer predicts that government forces will continue their offensive or will attack Huesca, and it is not impossible to turn the tide and gain the upper hand. Important developments are expected within a few weeks. At the same time, General Franco's offensive on Madrid has completely stalled, apparently due to a lack of troops. Associated Press reporter Miller is convinced that if the government forces can cut off Oviedo's transportation, General Mola will have to transfer troops from other locations to break through the government forces surrounding Oviedo. As for the residents of the city, they will suffer greatly, as Miller found that residents were already on the verge of starvation when he visited the area a month ago, and transportation has not yet been restored. French Defense Minister's Speech: International Peace; Arms Race Among Nations Equals Mad Suicide 77

Évreux, France Defense Minister Daladier recently gave a speech at a banquet of the local Radical Socialist Party branch, referring to the Anti-Comintern Pact between Germany and Japan, saying, "We now hear the strained voices from Asia. A nation in Asia now wants to take on the responsibility of defending Western culture. But we must tell all nations that the arms race is tantamount to mad suicide, because if another world war breaks out, human culture will be lost. We now wish to extend our hands of sincerity and friendship to all nations to help each other, but they should know that our hands are by no means weak and lifeless hands. Our country must be strong both materially and spiritually. Once France is weakened, the world will lose its peace, and our French people will also lose their freedom. Our French army is disciplined and strong. We are thorough pacifists, but we will never beg for peace." He then spoke about domestic affairs in France, saying, "Disturbing order, inciting public opinion, and empty rhetoric are all enemies of the republican system and democracy. It must be known that the order of a new society must be based on the internal peace of the French people. After the failure of the Social Democratic Republic in Germany, Hitler rose to power. After the collapse of democracy in Italy, Mussolini came to power. You should not have forgotten that. Domestic peace is a necessary condition for social progress, but there are other, more urgent conditions, and that is international peace. Today, swords are hanging all over the peace tree, and even in the olive groves, the glint of swords can be seen everywhere." (Note: Olive branches are a symbol of peace.) "I did not have this feeling at first, but the dictators of other countries have already said it many times. Our era is one where scientific developments are changing rapidly, and natural resources are abundant and inexhaustible. Therefore, the main issue we need to solve now is only the distribution of assets. We must now devote all our intelligence and strength to solving this problem, rather than engaging in futile struggles." (Havas, 29th)

Peiping: A Sideline Account of Aid to Suiyuan; Aid Suiyuan Associations and Student Fundraising 85

Throughout Peiping, counting all levels of schools from universities to elementary schools, along with other special schools, there are over ten thousand young students. In the past, these student groups have always been the vanguard of various movements. This holds true in the current Aid Suiyuan Movement. Since the official outbreak of the Suiyuan War, half a month has passed, and student groups have been rallying and calling for aid to Suiyuan for over ten days. Relying on their patriotic fervor and youthful courage, they have spared no effort in promoting the Aid Suiyuan Movement, as evidenced by hunger strikes and class boycotts, among other measures. Over the past ten days, the response from various sectors has generally been positive. However, in terms of actively rising up, spontaneously organizing groups, and joining forces with student groups to support the Aid Suiyuan Movement, as of now, the only participants have been the faculty and staff of cultural institutions and schools at various levels, along with a small number of women's groups. As such, organizations like the "All-Circles Aid Suiyuan Association," despite repeated calls from student groups, have remained in the preparatory stage and have not been formally established. This is partly due to the unique circumstances of Peiping, where people from all walks of life are more concerned about their personal and family assets than students. However, on the other hand, it can be reasoned that if the "skin is gone, where will the hair attach?" The Suiyuan War is a major turning point for the survival of the nation, a self-evident principle. According to general observations, people in various circles here still do not fully understand this principle, which is inferior to major southern cities. Currently, the main force behind the Aid Suiyuan Movement here is still supported solely by student groups. However, in reality, due to the limitations imposed by the authorities, schoolwork, and their own strength, it is a question worth noting how long this support can last. The biggest determining factor depends on the extent of the assistance provided to them by various circles, that is, whether organizations like the "All-Circles Aid Suiyuan Association" can be practically expanded and established.

Regarding all the expressions of students in this Aid Suiyuan Movement, there is much sympathy and support from all walks of life. However, regarding the matter of fundraising, there are several points that have aroused concerns from various parties. The former includes the so-called "five evils" of the Hebei-Chahar authorities, and the latter includes the Public Security Bureau's precautions against petty criminals posing as fundraisers, all of which are the most prominent. In addition, (1) the concern of all circles that they will be solicited for donations repeatedly without end; (2) the fear that the control and preservation of donations will not be in the hands of reliable people; (3) the inevitable confusion, duplication, and unnecessary phenomena in purchasing and sending goods to the front lines. This type of concern has more well-intentioned components and cannot be compared with fundamental distrust. Now, student groups have been able to observe these places and make corrections one by one. Once the facts are demonstrated, everything should not be a problem.

Class Boycotts and Symposiums 86

Since the launch of the Aid Suiyuan Movement, there have been two class boycotts in schools here. The first time, schools acted individually, without prior communication or subsequent notification. Therefore, in terms of order, there were differences in timing, and in terms of period, there were variations in length. Some lasted up to five days, while others lasted only half a day. The activities during the class boycotts also varied. The second class boycott was jointly decided by representatives from various schools. Except for a few schools that were unable to participate due to special difficulties or because the first class boycott lasted too long, the total number of schools participating in the second class boycott reached more than 20. The duration of this class boycott was uniformly two days, from the 25th to the 26th.

After representatives from various schools jointly decided on the class boycott, this resolution was separately approved by the entire student body of each school. During the two-day class boycott on the 25th and 26th, order was exceptionally good in each school. All work during the class boycott was entirely the responsibility of temporary organizations such as the "Working Committee During the Class Boycott." In addition to holding physical education inspections and smoke screen demonstrations, the most meaningful activity was the holding of symposiums.

During the class boycott, symposiums were held separately by each school on campus, and jointly expanded symposiums were held by various schools. The former were held on the 25th, and the situation in each school was exceptionally good. The topics of discussion were largely similar, such as "The Understanding and Our Tasks in the Suiyuan War of Resistance." School authorities and teachers participated in the speeches, with calm and enthusiastic attitudes, and tense but not impetuous emotions. These were the common points of each school. As for the results of their discussions, according to investigations conducted by reporters in various places, they were also largely consistent. In short, (1) the Suiyuan War is a key to the survival of the entire nation of China; (2) the ultimate goal of the Chinese people is to seek the freedom and equality of the entire nation, so we should do our best to support the current Suiyuan War. The expanded symposium jointly held by various schools on the 26th was held in three locations in the city, and the participants were very enthusiastic, and the order was also good. Professors from various schools were invited to give speeches, and the topic was "The Future of the Suiyuan War of Resistance." The opinions resulting from the discussions in the three locations were also relatively simple and consistent, that is, if our country can rise up and fight together, then the future should be able to achieve the thorough liberation of the nation.

The holding of this class boycott and symposium, not only the teachers and students of each school, but also the authorities took a tacit attitude and did not interfere, because with the support of national public opinion, there is no need to interfere as long as it does not go out of line, and there is no possibility of interference. As for the authorities of one or two schools, who have issued notices to admonish students, to obey the government, to unify steps, and not to disrupt the rear and distract the attention of the soldiers in front, they have been preventing students from acting excessively and preparing early. In fact, under the current situation, the goals are very simple, and there are probably no divergent or excessive actions. The actions of the authorities of a certain school are actually overconcerned. Indeed, after the two-day class boycott, all schools resumed classes on the 27th. This is a clear proof in fact.

War Service Corps 87

During this Suiyuan War, young students in Peiping, as in the past, were motivated by righteousness and joined the army in droves, attempting to participate in the war on the ground. Except for the seven young students from the four northeastern provinces who went there the other day, no others have been seen. Modern warfare is a complex matter that cannot be achieved with mere enthusiasm. Without long-term training, it may be a disservice. The "January 28th Incident" in Shanghai is a lesson from the past. Young students here seem to be fully aware of this. Furthermore, so-called combat requires the cooperation of both the front and rear to be called war. Recently, General Fu Zuoyi also earnestly stated this at a banquet for representatives from all walks of life. Therefore, most of the student work in Peiping this time seeks practicality. As for the "War Zone Service Corps" currently being organized, it is only a group organized after carefully examining the needs of the front line, which is very different from the purely righteous groups of the past. Therefore, the work they plan to do only includes the following items: (1) Rescue work; (2) Entertainment propaganda and condolence work; (3) Transportation and liaison work; (4) Various common technical work, such as radio, etc. Since the beginning of the preparation of this "War Zone Service Corps," many students from various schools have enthusiastically registered. If all the difficult problems can be solved smoothly, then the date of departure should not be far away.

Wang Yaqiao Assassinated in Wuzhou; Rumor is Wang Recently Fled to Wuzhou; Shot Three Times and Stabbed Twice; Three or Four Assailants All Fled 88

Hong Kong Correspondence: According to a visitor from Wuzhou, a major assassination occurred in Wuzhou on the 21st of this month at 11:00 PM. The incident took place at the rear residence of a certain address on Datong Middle Street, Datong Road, Wuzhou. A man was suddenly assassinated. The man was Wang Yaqiao, who recently fled to Guangxi Province, from another province. It is said that he once held a military position in a certain army. That evening, Wang was dining at a friend's residence when he was suddenly assassinated at 11:00 PM. Wang died on the spot, with three gunshot wounds and two stab wounds. After the incident, police detectives rushed to the scene to investigate, but the assailants had fled without a trace. The person who invited the deceased to dinner was also nowhere to be found. It is reported that the woman living in the residence brought her three children from Hong Kong on the 4th of this month (lunar calendar) and was currently residing at a certain address, which was also found by the deceased. The deceased and the woman were clearly acquainted. However, after the incident, the woman left behind her three children and Hong Kong currency and belongings, without taking any of them, and disappeared. At the time, neighbors heard five or six gunshots. After the police arrived at the scene, they learned that a major murder had occurred. Since the occurrence of this case, the entire Wuzhou police force has imposed a special curfew that night, cutting off traffic until dawn, but the assailants were not found. The mistress of the residence fled without a trace, and was obviously related to the case. The deceased was stabbed twice with a sword, which was still stuck in the body, it is said.

According to another message, an assassination occurred downstairs at a certain residence on Datong Road, Wuzhou. The murdered man was a man in his forties, shot three times, in a very tragic state. At the time, the police on duty nearby suddenly heard gunshots and rushed back to report to the branch office in charge. After investigating the residence, they learned that the deceased's name was Ren Shuren. A woman in her thirties had rented the house before the incident. After the incident, the woman had fled without a trace, apparently related to the case. It is said that there were three or four assailants. According to the landlord, the woman had just arrived from Hong Kong and had only moved in three days before the incident occurred. Wuzhou authorities considered this case serious and seemed to involve political revenge, and are investigating it strictly.

Guangdong Province Actively Purchases Silver; Provincial Bank Continuously Increases Issuance of Silver Yuan Notes; Simultaneously Uses Legal Tender as Reserve Fund 89

Guangzhou Correspondence: To meet the need for supply and accelerate the purchase of silver as much as possible, the Guangdong Provincial Bank has been continuously issuing the silver yuan notes of the Provincial Bank that have been printed but not yet issued in recent days. It was verified that 2 million yuan worth of one-yuan silver yuan notes were signed and issued on the 25th. On the 26th, five-yuan and ten-yuan silver yuan notes that were printed and stored were continuously issued, but the amount was not announced. It is reported that the reserve fund for this issuance is 40% in bonds of the bank and 60% in national currency obtained from the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications. The first batch of 15 million yuan of national currency and the second batch of 10 million yuan will also be transported. The Provincial Bank will use the obtained national currency to exchange for Provincial silver yuan notes from the Guangzhou Branch of the Reserve Fund Management Committee at full value, and use the national currency to offset the Provincial bed reserve. Yesterday, the Provincial Bank officially announced the issuance of new silver yuan notes, stating that the bank's stock of Provincial notes was very small, and that people have been flocking to the bank and its branches to sell silver. Without issuing new notes, it would be difficult to cope. Therefore, the legal tender was sent to the Guangzhou Branch of the Reserve Fund Management Committee for verification and collection, and new Provincial notes printed by the US banknotes company were exchanged, which were still signed by Chairman Song (Ziliang) of the branch and President Gu Yiqun and Deputy President Yun Zhaokun. Before Chairman Song signed, the president and deputy president first signed 2 million yuan of two-yuan notes for the need to purchase silver. If a certain amount of silver is purchased, then a certain amount of new notes will be issued according to a two-to-one ratio, in order to complete the purchase of silver as soon as possible, and to ensure the Provincial note reserve. The Provincial Bank issued another announcement on the 27th, stating that the number of people selling silver has continued to increase in recent days, and the previous amount of notes has been exhausted. It is necessary to continue signing and issuing notes to meet the needs. The ten-yuan and five-yuan notes will be jointly signed by Chairman Song of the Guangzhou Branch of the Reserve Fund Management Committee and the President and Deputy President of the bank, and will be issued from the 27th of this month. The bank hereby informs all sectors that all taxes and market transactions will be conducted in the same manner as the Provincial notes signed by former President Shen. According to the bank's estimate, the total amount of currency needed in the province is tens of millions of yuan. Previously, the bank issued a total of 24,108,000 yuan of silver yuan notes, and the bank's cash reserve totaled 12,462,000 yuan. In the future, while increasing the issuance of silver yuan notes, it will also increase the reserve fund to avoid the abuses of excessive issuance.

Fengjing: Younger Brother Murders Elder Brother for Inheritance 90

Shen Rongchu, a 56-year-old resident of the 2nd neighborhood, 2nd district of the northern city of this county, was attacked at noon on the 26th of this month by his cousin, Liu Chu (51 years old), along with his son Zuyin, nephew Hongnian, and more than ten others. They claimed to want to reclaim the documents and re-divide the family property. Shen's younger brother was also imprisoned. When Shen's father passed away, the family property was divided into three shares, and documents were established at that time. However, Liu Chu's share had already been spent. Therefore, he recently had a whimsical idea, claiming that it was his aunt's intention to request a re-division. Shen Rongchu and others refused, and a dispute arose. It is now heard that Shen Rongchu has decided to hire a lawyer to file a criminal lawsuit against his brother for his actions.

Suzhou: Commencement of Second Installment of Land Tax 91

The Wuxian County Government has been ordered to collect land tax. The first installment of 40% was commenced earlier, and the second installment of 60% is scheduled to commence today (1st) for a period of two months. A late payment fine of 3% will be added for overdue payments. The county government believes that this year's rice harvest is abundant, so there is no reduction in this year's land tax, and the full amount will be collected. However, various landowners and shopkeepers argue that although the autumn harvest is abundant, some villages, such as Weiting, are still barren. Therefore, they are still striving to request a reduction of 10% to show compassion, but it is feared that it will be difficult to achieve their goal. As for this year's rent, although there has been a slight improvement in recent days, the amount collected is only a little over 10%. The county government is currently devising methods to urge collection.

Major Theft Case; Rigorously Arresting the Mastermind 92

A major theft case occurred at Dafeng Silver Furnace in Lüyuan Nei months ago, with stolen gold bars and silver ornaments worth approximately 100,000 yuan. Shareholders of the shop, with acting manager Ji Yushu and bookkeeper Xia Buzhou, suspected of embezzlement, sued the court. The court has already sentenced Ji Yushu and Xia Buzhou to criminal penalties, and the case is now on appeal. A few days ago, there was a new development in the case. Ji Yushu reported to the detective team that Xia Likuan, the instigator of the case, had been captured. There were also two perpetrators, Bai and others, hiding in Shanghai. The detective team sent officers to Shanghai to arrest them, but they were not found. The detective team escorted Xia Likuan to the Public Security Bureau on the 30th for detention and interrogation. However, this case is of great importance, and Director Zhang paid close attention to whether there was a background. On the one hand, he is arresting Bai and others to investigate the case.

Wuxi: Enthusiastic Contributions to Support Suiyuan 93

The contribution to the nation and the Aid Suiyuan Movement have been quite enthusiastic in this county. Large Quantities of Grain Leaving the Country 94

Recently, the grain transported by the railway station of this county to the Jinpu and Longhai Railways is stacked in the open air, in addition to the existing warehouses are full, due to the lack of vehicles. Although the Ministry of Railways has repeatedly dispatched vehicles to Wuxi, they are still insufficient for loading and transportation. At present, most merchants have contacted the Shanghai Steamship Bureau to load the goods from the interior to Shanghai, and then transport them from Shanghai to Yantai, and then transfer them to the Longhai Railway. However, the date of arrival is three or four days later than by train. I sincerely hope that the authorities will pay attention to it in order to maintain the people's livelihood.

Commencement of Second Installment of Land Tax 95

According to the provincial order, the second installment of land tax for the 25th year in this county is collected at the rate of 4 jiao, 4 fen, and 3 hao per mu of flat land for provincial tax, 9 fen and 4 li and 4 hao for county tax, 4 jiao and blank li and 6 hao for county surtax, and 2 fen and 6 li and 7 hao for collection fees, for a total of 9 jiao, 6 fen, and 6 li. In addition to the first installment of 43% of 8 fen 6 li and 4 hao collected first, the second installment is 6 jiao, 5 fen, 7 li and 9 hao. In addition, a protection regiment donation of 2 fen is collected for each string. The county government issued a notice yesterday, setting December 1st as the commencement date, with a deadline of two months for completion. A late payment fine of 3% will be added to the total amount of provincial and county surtaxes due after the deadline. If it is still blank by the end of the year, a blank fine of blank will be added.

Danyang: Continued Account of the Mingfeng School Disturbance 100

The Director of Instruction of Mingfeng Elementary School, Zhu Menglian, was suspended from her position by the Education Bureau. The students went to the Education Bureau to petition for her reinstatement, but to no avail, which led to a disturbance in which the students expelled the principal, Hao Shuying, and the new Director of Instruction, Zhang Fang blank. At the same time, the Education Bureau, based on Principal Hao's report that the disturbance was instigated by Zhu Menglian and teachers Wei Anshi and Shen Huaizhu, and that students had held meetings at Zhu Menglian's home beforehand, reported the situation to the County Government and arrested Zhu Menglian and others that night. A notice was posted, stating that the school would be temporarily suspended for reorganization before reopening. Yesterday morning, the students of the school went to school, but seeing that the school gate was closed, they gathered again and went to the Education Bureau to petition for classes. Upon hearing the report, the County Government, in order to thoroughly investigate the facts of the disturbance, personally led the bailiffs to the Education Bureau and selected the five oldest students who came to petition, Zhou Deyuan, Zheng Zengxiang, Zhou Fulong, Liu Zhaoxing, and Liu Yongkang, and brought them to the County Government along with Zhu Menglian and others blank and handed them over to the judiciary for handling. In the afternoon, Judge Liu Chengshen presided over the trial, and as a result, Zhu Menglian blank and thirteen others were detained. The students Zhou Deyuan and others were temporarily held in the waiting room, pending investigation.

Ningbo: Heroic Woman Resists Robbers to Save Father-in-Law 101

He Yufa, an old farmer from Heshai, Younan, who had some savings, was coveted by bandits. At about 11 p.m. on the 20th, six or seven bandits suddenly came, destroyed the door, broke into his home, twisted Yufa, pressed a pistol against his chest, and forced him to hand over his property. His daughter-in-law, Ms. Ma, in her early twenties, was brave by nature. Seeing her father-in-law being coerced by the robbers, she disregarded her own safety and stepped forward to seize the bandit's pistol. Yufa was able to take the opportunity to escape. However, Ms. Ma was stabbed five times in the back of her hand with a knife by another bandit while fighting with the bandit for the pistol. She could not bear the pain and released her hand. Because Yufa went out, fearing that the police would be called, the bandits fled together, so the loss was still small.

Yarn Flowers: Current Yarn Heading to Sichuan, Futures Market Sees Sudden Surge in Buying, Batch Closings Have No Impact 102

The yarn market is soaring, with a fierce momentum fueled by brisk sales, a shortage of current yarn at factories, and eager buying from customers unable to find goods to meet their demands. This has stirred excitement, leading to a buying frenzy and a sharp rise in market prices. However, some industry players are closing out batches, and Indian merchants are also seen selling, but this has been unable to halt the upward trend. In reality, this is still due to the robust spot market business, but the price increases have not been too drastic.

Recently, yarn prices have risen by more than five yuan. At the opening of the futures market, all months experienced a uniform surge, displaying immense momentum. This was primarily due to Sichuan merchants purchasing one to two thousand bales of current yarn the previous afternoon. Furthermore, it was reported that 1,000 bales of 20-count Jincheng Double Deer yarn from the Yong'an factory, scheduled for delivery in November, were entirely bought up by Sichuan merchants. This news shook the market, causing the December futures to jump three yuan, and the distant months to rise by one to two yuan. News spread quickly that yarn sales were brisk, and the eagerness to acquire spot yarn in the market was particularly strong. As factories struggled to supply current yarn, the market continued its upward trajectory. Consequently, all months saw a price increase ranging from 3.40 to 4.80 yuan compared to the previous day's closing price. At the afternoon opening, it was reported that spot yarn trading had improved, and market sentiment remained positive. However, major players sold off batches, which slightly calmed the market. As a result, prices for all months rose by an additional 0.30 to 0.80 yuan compared to the morning's closing price. Senkang and Runkang engaged in buying in the morning and selling in the afternoon. The cotton market is stable, and market conditions are not as strong as those of the yarn market. Piece Goods: Strong Demand from Cloth Merchants, Prices in Various Regions Gradually Approaching Shanghai Market, Scarcity of Spot Goods Prevents Sales from Expanding 105

Yesterday, the cotton cloth market was characterized by firm and active market conditions. The supply of goods was strong, and the shortage continued to worsen. Consequently, market sentiment was steady, and sales prices in various regions were also rebounding rapidly due to brisk sales. Compared to the Shanghai market, prices were already in line. Therefore, the eagerness to purchase increased, leading to fierce competition for spot goods. As a result, spot goods in the market became even scarcer. Furthermore, with the recent surge of five yuan in near-month cotton yarn prices, and the shortage and high prices of spot yarn, the prices of various colors and types of plain cloth rose uniformly. White cloth from Chinese factories and British Jardine Matheson factories increased by 1.2 jiao per piece. Eastern fine cloth, fine twill, grey cloth, and coarse cloth increased by 0.05 to 0.1 jiao per piece. Local fine twill increased by 0.1 to 0.15 jiao per piece. Blue cloth and bleached cloth increased by 0.1 jiao. Serge, Zhigong, line fabrics, and printed fabrics all increased by 0.0025 to 0.005 yuan per yard. Velvet goods, white twill velvet, and striped velvet were in high demand and selling quickly. Spot goods were in urgent need, and occasionally sold for an additional 0.2 yuan per piece. Sales of colored cloth were also gradually improving. Yesterday, Sichuan merchants absorbed over 200 pieces of blue cloth, colored twill, Zhigong, and line fabrics, while inland merchants absorbed over 400 pieces of various types of coarse cloth, which was a relatively large amount. Due to the scarcity of spot goods, the transaction volume remained difficult to increase.

Double-Faced Yellow Camel Wool Declines in Price Due to High Inventory 106

The favorable conditions of the woolen market were detailed in previous reports. Unexpectedly, the price of yellow camel wool suddenly declined yesterday. Double-faced yellow camel wool has been popular recently, with many men's and women's overcoats using it. It is also used for linings. Therefore, last winter, supply could not meet demand, and prices soared, allowing distributors to profit greatly. However, this year, arrivals have doubled, and there are many Japanese goods. Many woolen businesses have been distributing it, but sales have been slow, and prices have fallen. Yesterday, ordinary first-grade thick yellow camel wool was reduced by 4.4 yuan per batch, and slightly thinner second-grade wool was reduced by 3.75 yuan per batch.

The gold market yesterday saw some selling interest from spot dealers, while buyers remained on the sidelines and observed. After the opening, spot dealers continued to show selling interest, triggering a selling trend. Grains: Flour Delivery Settled Privately 110

Since the flour delivery was changed from the exchange to the public warehouse, the procedures have become more complicated. Therefore, before the end of the month, both parties settled privately, so there was no official delivery. As for the flour trend, November was relatively calm, and there was no significant change in prices. However, looking ahead, prices may gradually rise again. This is because there are fewer wheat arrivals, and Shaanxi merchants are restocking, so wheat shipments from the north are bound to decrease. Furthermore, the only hope, foreign wheat, is also gradually rising. Yesterday's prices reported that Chicago was up 0.4-0.5 yuan, Canada was up 0.2-0.3 yuan, and Liverpool was up 0.1375 yuan. All of these factors seem to favor long positions, and the background is inevitably related to military affairs.

Abundant Arrivals of Late Season Indica Rice from the Yangtze River 112

Yesterday's market for late-season indica rice continued to soften due to abundant arrivals. Shipments from various ports in Jiangxi, Hunan, Shahan, and others totaled more than 20,000 bags per day. The market seemed likely to continue to decline, but merchants from Guangdong and Shantou suddenly became active. Shantou merchants purchased 3,000 bags of various types of rice, and Guangdong merchants purchased 4,000 bags of various types of coarse and broken rice. The market immediately rebounded, and the decline slowed. Beiyang merchants in this street also accommodated several hundred bags of each type. Therefore, while Yuan rice and other types saw a small price decline, coarse and other types of rice were able to hold steady. The opening price for Gan rice was more than 3,000 bags, for Xiang rice it was more than 4,000 bags, and for Yongtai machine-milled Yuan rice it was more than 400 bags.

Weak Sales Continue, Thin Rice Falls Continuously 113

(Shanghai South) Yesterday, arrivals from various merchants totaled over 100, with a total of more than 22,300 shi of goods. Thin rice still accounted for 60-70 merchants, but the desire for thin rice remained sluggish. Merchants from Pingjin Qingyan and other regions only purchased more than 6,000 bags, and they all selected high-quality goods. Mid-range goods seemed to be rejected unless they were particularly good, leading to a continued softening of the market. As a result, high-quality goods fell slightly by 0.07 yuan, while mid-range goods fell by 0.1-0.02 yuan. Thick粳 rice sales amounted to over 700 bags, which was still acceptable, so prices did not change much. Du jian had an oversupply, so prices were reduced slightly by 0.05 yuan. Yang jian had no transactions. Yin yuan remained stagnant and prices also fell by a few yuan.

Local News

Metals: Eastern White Iron Unusually Expensive 118

The market for Eastern white iron has been very brisk for the past few days. This is because factories, seeing that the price of black iron sheets (used as the base for white iron) has risen sharply, have also increased their selling prices in this port. Yesterday, 3-foot by 7-foot sheets sold for $1.20 each, a dime more than before, and 3-foot by 6-foot sheets sold for $1.00 each, also seven or eight cents more than before. Recently, buyers have been making every effort to purchase, while factories are restricting sales and unwilling to easily release goods. It seems likely that the market will continue to improve. It is reported that a total of seven or eight thousand sheets were sold in the market yesterday and the day before. However, the lowest quoted price was $1.12 or $1.13 for 7-foot sheets, and $0.92 or $0.93 for 6-foot sheets. Current transactions are not at these prices, and sellers are unwilling to let go of their goods.

Pig Lead Prices Reach Peak 119

The price of pig lead reached $31 per picul yesterday, the highest price in more than a decade. Bulk transactions were relatively quiet, but scattered sales were still taking place. It is said that overseas prices have recently risen sharply, and inventories in this port are low, so it is feared that prices will be difficult to bring down.

Page 12

Oil Market: Hankou and Shanghai Turpentine Supplies Both Interrupted; Jiaxing New Oil Only 10% of Normal Yield; Hankou Old Oil Almost Completely Collected 120

The turpentine market is extremely unusual. Turpentine in both Hankou and Shanghai has long been collected by foreign firms. Hankou relies on new Macheng oil, which can be transported by carts, with dozens of shipments arriving every day or every other day, all of which are eagerly pre-ordered by various groups. However, it is unknown how many people are eagerly awaiting supplies. Such a large market has been interrupted for half a month, and there is still no definite date for new supplies to arrive, which is unprecedented since the opening of the market. The yield of new Jingzhou oil is still abundant, but it is usually only available after winter, so it is not expected to be used to supplement supplies at this time. However, the old oil production areas have not yet shipped everything out, as upstream waters are shallow and obstructed. It is said that "you can hear the ladder ringing, but you can't see anyone coming down the stairs." The situation in Hankou is as described above.

The interruption in Shanghai has also lasted for two weeks. Each year, at the time of new production, it relies on the nearby Jiaxing oil transported by local carts to supplement supplies. According to this year's yield, it is only 10% of normal. Last year, new oil production could reach 60,000 pieces, but this winter only 6,000 pieces can be produced, and the quoted price has risen to $8.55 or $8.60 per dan. This is equivalent to a new oil cost of about $27 per market scale. The oil mills are only accumulating and not selling, waiting for a better price in the future. However, there are still more than 10,000 pieces of old oil, but they are all in the hands of speculators, who are increasingly unwilling to sell as prices rise, which is equivalent to having no goods. The inventory of carting companies is very low. It is said they must sell for $26. The output in Jinhua and Lanxi in eastern Zhejiang is about to peak, but there has been too much selling. The daily production has to be used to settle forward oil contracts, so current sales are also limited. Furthermore, the combined price to ship to Shanghai must be above $23, and there are still no goods for sale. Foreign firms are still continuing to purchase, but no further deals have been heard since the price passed $24 per pound, so it is feared that prices will not approach this level for some time. Foreign firms in Hankou and Yichang have already sold a lot. Before summing up accounts, the oil produced was used to settle with foreign firms, leaving very little remaining. Therefore, foreign firms will not trade again until February or March. According to news from Hankou, Shanghai foreign firms have already purchased, for delivery in a few months, with two or three hundred tons in transactions, but there is no such saying in this port, so it must be investigated further to confirm.

Excessive Drop in River Water Level; White Tung Oil Supply Delayed; Abundant Production, Beware of Small Market in Future 121

More than two months have passed since the new tung oil production began. The foreign firms sold in Hankou are all current oil during the transition between new and old oil, and the quantities are scattered. Therefore, although transactions continue intermittently, the impact on the market is minimal. What can change the market is the large number of forward oil contracts. Roughly speaking, the amount sold at that time for November was not much, so exports this month are not strong. Although the market sometimes experiences ups and downs, the overall trend is that price fluctuations are minimal. It is fortunate that this is the case, because the Yangtze River water level is extremely shallow. If exports were slightly stronger, it would inevitably be insufficient to meet demand. It is unknown what the scene would be if the current oil supply were short. According to the current supply in Hankou, it can only be used for foreign firms to replenish a small amount of current delivery. If the delivery of a large number of forward oil contracts is due next month, and the water remains shallow and delayed, and the arrival of goods is still as scattered as it is now, a large shortage of current oil is inevitable. Therefore, Hankou firms stopped selling forward oil to foreign firms on December 1, and recently all sales have been for February. The highest price sold was $50 per ton, then $49.50, and then $49. The yield in Sichuan, Hunan, and Hubei this year is abundant, so people were originally very happy. The reason why prices cannot fall now is actually because the supply is blocked by shallow water. When transportation becomes convenient, there will inevitably be a day when goods flood in. Therefore, merchants are willing to sell forward contracts at a lower price. Since the establishment of vegetable oil factories in this port, tung oil has been the first type of oil to be produced. Although it is said to specialize in refining, it also engages in foreign trade. It is reported that more than 100 tons have been purchased in Hankou and are currently being tested, with gradual efforts to expand. Foreign firms selling refined oil must have it refined by this factory, with a fixed refining fee of 8 jiao per ton. However, at present, it is only used for oil produced in Zhejiang Province and has not yet been popularized for use in Hunan, Hubei, and other provinces. As for Zhejiang tung oil, as the origin has sold forward oil in advance, the current production can only be used to settle current goods, so the current oil is very popular. The price per cwt must be $47.68 for Shanghai delivery, and only a few orders can be taken, also because the water level of the Qiantang River is shallow, and the arrival of goods is not convenient for loading and transportation.

Soybean Oil and Peanut Oil Prices Expected to Rise 122

Recently, the market prices of soybean oil and peanut oil have risen because the northern region has entered the river freezing season, causing all roads to rush shipments. Production prices have risen daily, and it is said that Qingdao will increase export taxes, so the market is excited. The price of Niuzhuang soybean oil has reached $23, and the situation is still tense. Yesterday, the market opened with 200 pieces of local factory soybean oil, 250 pieces of Niuzhuang soybean oil, 50 pieces of Dalian soybean oil, 100 pieces of Dalian Qishan soybean oil, 100 pieces of Yantai Qishan soybean oil, 200 pieces of Qingdao Qishan soybean oil, 100 pieces of Bo'er peanut oil, 200 pieces of Jiacang raw oil, 100 pieces of Qingpi raw oil, and 100 pieces of Jiaozhou transported raw oil. Prices have increased by 3 jiao compared to the previous market.

Comfort Mission Telegraphs Overseas Chinese to Raise Funds to Aid Wounded Soldiers and Refugees; Chiang and Yan Both Send Telegrams of Condolences 123

The Suiyuan Anti-Bandit Comfort and Relief Association, jointly formed by the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the Local Self-Government Association, and the Red Cross Society, yesterday telegraphed the Overseas Chinese Chamber of Commerce, asking them to raise funds to aid wounded soldiers and refugees. The news is recorded below:

Telegram to Overseas Chinese

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the Local Self-Government Association, and the Red Cross Society telegraphed the Chinese Chambers of Commerce in Singapore and the Philippines yesterday, saying: "The Suiyuan War has expanded, and the whole country is united. However, wounded soldiers and refugees urgently need relief. Medicine and cold-weather supplies must be purchased in Shanghai. We have now jointly formed a Comfort and Relief Association to raise funds and manage them in a unified manner, so that money is not wasted and things are done effectively. We hope that your association will make efforts to raise funds and remit them at any time. We sincerely hope for this." The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the Local Self-Government Association, and the Red Cross Society kowtow respectfully.

Telegrams from Various Parties

(1) Telegram from Chairman Chiang: "Received your telegram with gratitude. I am very pleased to know that you have arrived safely in Shanghai. Chiang Kai-shek (seal)." (2) Telegram from Yan Xishan: "Received your telegram with gratitude. You have made a special trip, and the hospitality was inadequate. You braved the wind to return south, and your efforts are appreciated. The front line needs assistance, and we are grateful for your concern and will do our best to raise funds. The soldiers will be deeply moved when they hear this. Special reply and thanks. Yan Xishan (seal)." (3) Public note to the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the Local Self-Government Association, and the Red Cross Society: "Received your respectful telegram. The gentlemen representing your association recently came to our province to express condolences and inspect. We deeply regret that the hospitality was inadequate, and we are ashamed. We will work hard together to overcome the national crisis. We are inspired by your leadership and offer our respect. Special telegram reply. Yan Xishan and Zhao Daiwen (seal)."

Various Parties Actively Support Suiyuan Movement; Salt Revenue Audit Office Donates 10,000; Lu Bohong Asks Shareholders to Provide Local Relief; Donations from All Walks of Life Flow in Eagerly 124

Zhu Tingqi, Director-General of the Salt Revenue Audit Office of the Ministry of Finance, has now specially donated $10,000 to be forwarded to Chairman Fu of Suiyuan by Minister of Finance Kong to provide comfort. Two telegrams are recorded below: (1) Zhu's presentation to Finance Minister Kong: "I have investigated that the Mongol bandits have invaded Suiyuan, and the National Army has launched a large-scale crusade, with frequent reports of victory, and the seas are rejoicing. Now, all parties are donating money and assistance, and responding in unison. Our office and its staff across the country have jointly donated $10,000 to express our condolences. I respectfully submit this to Your Excellency, and I beg you to forward it to Chairman Fu of Suiyuan for inspection and forwarding to the front lines. I earnestly pray. Sincerely." (2) Kong's telegraph to Suiyuan to Chairman Fu Yizhi: "The bandit-Mongol invasion has angered the whole country. I deeply admire your loyalty and courage in defending the country. The staff of our Ministry of Finance's Salt Revenue Audit Office has presented a donation of $10,000. I have specially remitted it through Yuhua Bank. Please check and collect it. Together with the previously remitted $20,000, use it to prepare leather clothing for the officers and soldiers." Various important news items are also recorded below.

Lu Bohong's Telegram

"The domestic community is deeply angered by the Mongol bandit invasion of Suiyuan. Although the bandit's lair has been overcome, the number of wounded soldiers on our front line is gradually increasing, and the need for relief work is very urgent." Lu Bohong, a leader of the Shanghai Catholic Church and a great philanthropist, has joined the Red Cross Society and the Charity Relief Committee in the name of the Catholic Association to assist in the work. In addition, he has launched a fundraising campaign among Catholics, appointing his son Yin Gengjun to be responsible for liaison and purchasing medical supplies to transport to the front. At the same time, he has telegraphed the Central Hospital in Peiping to send doctors and nurses with medicines to work in Suiyuan. Various Charitable Organizations Establish Joint Relief Association Yesterday - Announce Purpose, Pass Articles of Association, Elect Chairman and Staff 125

The Shanghai Charitable Organizations Joint Relief Association held its inaugural meeting at Renji Hall yesterday at 3 p.m. Representatives present included Kong Xiangxi (represented by Chen Liting), Wu Tiecheng (represented by Li Dachao), Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yiting, Zhang Xiaolin, Qu Wenliu, Li Dachao, Yu Zuoting, Mao Yun, Pan Gongzhan, Cao Yunxiang, Zhu Ziqiao (represented by Tao Fuqing), Zhao Jinqing, Cheng Jingsheng, Huang Hanzhi, Guan Jiongzhi, Cai Jinjun (represented by Yin Guanzhi), Pan Xulun, Zhang Binghui, Zhu Shaoping, Lu Bohong, as well as Yuan Ying of the Chinese Buddhist Association, Chen Tiesheng of the Chinese Child Welfare Association, Chen Zhuangbao of the Chinese Leprosy Relief Association, Wang Xiafu of the Chinese Women and Children Relief Association, Zhang Lanping of the Chinese Red Swastika Society, Wang Tongzhang of the Renyi Shan Society, Feng Yangshan of the Chinese Jisheng Society, Xu Qianlin of the Chinese Moral Society, Shen Jianhou of the Puji Shan Society, Zhan Xiguang of the Boji Shan Society, Weng Yinchu of the Lianyi Shan Society, Cui Fuzhuang of the Zhisheng Shanyuan, Jiang Maoshuo of the Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Red Cross Society, Fan Kaitai of the Yiji Shan Society, Ye Shouhai of the Xin Puyu Tang, and over a hundred others.

Chairman's Report

First, Qu Wenliu was elected as temporary chairman. Mr. Qu stood up and reported on the purpose of establishing the association, stating in brief that this time, the border regions were disturbed by the pseudo-bandits, causing immense suffering. Especially during this severely cold weather, soldiers are defending the country and resisting the war in freezing conditions, and the people are suffering from cold and hunger. Therefore, charitable people from Shanghai are gathered to establish this association to promote disaster relief efforts in the border regions, in order to fulfill the duty of our people in the rear. He then reported that the Zhenwu Committee had agreed to allocate 100,000 yuan in public bonds for the association's disaster relief efforts. Master Yingguang also donated over 1,500 yuan of conversion money to the association.

Preparatory Process

After the chairman's report, Li Dachao reported on the preparatory process of the association, stating that the national defense gateway is currently disturbed by the pseudo-Mongolian bandit army, and the soldiers at the front are bravely resisting. We in the rear should enthusiastically contribute, as it is said, "Seeing what is right, act courageously, and a benevolent person will not yield." Then, Wang Xiaolai reported on his trip to Suiyuan and Chahar, stating that our country, both the government and the people, must protect the integrity of the national territory, the integrity of politics, and the integrity of the military. Under unified command, we will resist the war to the end. Today's government is not the government of the past, and today's people are not the people of the past. The establishment of this association is to demonstrate the power of the people.

Discussion of Proposals

After the reports, discussions began: (1) Passed the Purpose of the Shanghai Charitable Organizations Joint Relief Association; (2) Passed the Articles of Association of the Shanghai Charitable Organizations Joint Relief Association; (3) Passed all representatives attending the inaugural meeting as members of the association; (4) Passed the chairman, vice-chairman, standing committee members, and heads and deputy heads of each group of the association; (5) Resolved that the specific plan for disaster relief by the association be submitted to the Standing Committee for review and implementation.

Purpose of Disaster Relief

The purpose of the Shanghai Charitable Organizations Joint Relief Association states: "Recently, the national crisis has become increasingly serious. Suiyuan is an important town in our northwest border defense, and war has already broken out. Fortunately, the soldiers at the front are fulfilling their duty to protect the country and defend the people, bravely fighting and frequently reporting victories. However, we must remember that the area is inherently bitterly cold, and now it is severe winter. Suffering this calamity, in the freezing conditions, under the rain of bullets and guns, the number of displaced and dead people is simply unknown. The charitable organizations of Shanghai have always enthusiastically engaged in disaster relief efforts. Now that the compatriots in the war zone are crying out under the blades of weapons, how can we bear to sit idly by? We should work together with one heart and devote ourselves to the duty of rescue and care. Saving the country and saving people is also saving ourselves. We, the colleagues, are based on this principle to organize this association, deeply hoping to gather great spirit and strength for the common cause of relief, according to the direction of the incident, to the extent of our ability, in order to boost the morale of the people and promote the prestige of the country. People from all walks of life, stirred by righteous indignation, naturally have sympathy. We hope that they will enthusiastically support and donate generously, strive forward, enthusiastically serve, share the same boat, and make concerted efforts. We present these sincere words and humbly request your consideration."

Full Text of Articles of Association

Articles of Association of the Shanghai Charitable Organizations Joint Relief Association: Article 1: This association is jointly organized by various charitable organizations and enthusiastic supporters, with the purpose of handling disaster relief matters in the disaster areas. It is named the Shanghai Charitable Organizations Joint Relief Association. Article 2: In addition to individual members, any organization joining in the name of an organization may elect one to three people as representatives for each organization member. Article 3: The committee of this association is organized by a number of members elected by the general meeting of members. Article 4: The committee should elect a number of standing committee members to preside over all daily affairs of the association. Article 5: The standing committee members shall elect one chairman, one vice-chairman, and a number of standing resident committee members. Article 6: When necessary, the association may establish various special committees, and the detailed rules for their operation shall be separately formulated. Article 7: The work of the association is divided into the following groups: (1) General Affairs Group, (2) Relief Group, (3) Fundraising Group, (4) Finance Group, (5) Audit Group. The detailed rules for the operation of each group shall be separately formulated. Article 8: Each group shall have one director and several deputy directors, who shall be concurrently appointed from the standing committee members or members. Each group shall have several staff members to handle the affairs of the group, who shall be appointed by the Standing Committee from the staff of various charitable organizations or other enthusiastic supporters. If the affairs of each group are heavy, they may be divided into sections, each with one section chief. When necessary, a deputy section chief may be established, both of whom shall be filled by staff members. Article 9: The committee members, directors, etc. of this association are all voluntary positions. Employees may be given living expenses as appropriate. If they are transferred from various charitable organizations, they shall still be paid by their original organizations. Article 10: The funds of this association shall be raised separately by organization members and individual members. Article 11: The general meeting of members and the committee of this association shall be convened by the standing committee. Article 12: The standing committee shall be convened by the chairman and vice-chairman at any time. Article 13: The income and expenditure of funds and materials of this association, in addition to being published in a separate report booklet, shall also be announced in newspapers at any time. Article 14: The association shall establish an office at Renji Tang, Yunnan Road, Shanghai. Article 15: These articles of association shall be implemented after being approved by the general meeting of members. Any matters not covered shall be revised by the committee.
