Wang Chonghui Discusses That World War Is Closer - Possible Outbreak at Any Time - Italy Seems to Officially Recognize Manchukuo - League of Nations Should Make a Solemn Statement 126

Following the successive signing of the Japan-Germany and Japan-Italy agreements, the international community is divided into two major fronts, and the situation is more tense than before. A reporter from the Shenshi News Agency specially visited Mr. Wang Chonghui, member of the Central Supervisory Committee, on the morning of the 30th, and he kindly made a statement.

World War - Outbreak is Faster

The Second World War is imminent. Although the Spanish war appears on the surface to be an internal conflict in Spain, in fact, the government army and the revolutionary army have international backgrounds, and each has other countries behind them providing assistance. In reality, it is no different from an international war. Since Japan, Germany, and Italy have successively signed agreements, the front lines of the international war have become increasingly clear, and the outbreak of the Second World War is also faster. Now, all countries in the world are uniformly stepping up military preparations, and the danger of war has reached its peak. An outbreak is possible at any time. Once an unexpected international event occurs, such as the event of the First World War, then the war will occur.

League of Nations - Prestige Is Difficult to Recover

The League of Nations now has absolutely no prestige to sanction and maintain peace. The biggest reason is that the power of public opinion in the world cannot match military power. For example, in the case of Italy's invasion of Abyssinia, most of the public opinion around the world sympathized with Abyssinia. European and American authoritative journalists all loudly attacked Italy, but in fact, it was ultimately difficult to match military power. Although the League of Nations passed economic sanctions by its member states, it was of no avail because Italy had already purchased military supplies before the war, resulting in no results. In addition, the League of Nations' procedures are too cumbersome, which is also a reason for losing prestige. After the incident occurs, it must go through lengthy procedures such as investigation, research, and meetings, which is of no help. Moreover, no matter what, it is difficult to match military power. Therefore, it is difficult for the League of Nations to restore its prestige in fact. The League of Nations has now established a reform committee to engage in reforming the League of Nations' organization. However, since Japan, Germany, and other countries have withdrawn from the League of Nations, it is not easy to restore prestige.

Italy Recognizes Manchukuo - Should Have a Statement

The cooperation between Germany and Italy with Japan is entirely for the European aspect, while Japan is for the Asian aspect. It has a considerable impact on China, but the impact on Soviet Russia should be even greater. The relationship between China and Italy has always been good. This time, Italy cooperated with Japan due to its own interests, which is quite unexpected. However, Italy has not yet withdrawn from the League of Nations. It has been telegraphed for days that Italy recognizes Manchukuo in exchange with Japan for recognition of Italy's annexation of Abyssinia. If Italy officially expresses its recognition of Manchukuo, then I (Wang said himself) think that the League of Nations should have a solemn statement, because the League of Nations has not yet recognized Manchukuo. If a member state openly recognizes it, the League of Nations should naturally have a solemn statement.

Our Country Should Seek - Self-Reliance and Revival

The international situation is becoming increasingly serious, and the fate of the Chinese nation is becoming even more precarious. On this path of survival, we have no other way but to seek self-reliance and revival, because international relations are all based on the interests of the country, and there is no such thing as justice and friendship. If we have strong national strength, we can cooperate with other countries and seek true friendship, he said.

Ministry of Industry and Commerce's Bureau of Foreign Trade Plans to Improve Domestic Fruits - Control Production and Revitalize Rural Areas 127

In recent years, because countries around the world have generally felt economic panic, they have dumped domestic surpluses abroad, with our country as the final recipient. As for fruit, our country's annual output is also huge, but farmers adhere to old methods, leading to gradual decline. Foreign businessmen take the opportunity to rise, resulting in our country's imports of fruit reaching a total value of 6.5 million yuan last year, according to customs statistics. Apples accounted for 500,000 yuan, with American goods being the most, accounting for six-tenths of the total. Japan, Taiwan, Australia, and Canada were next. Raisin imports also reached 500,000 yuan. Orange imports reached 1.5 million yuan, also with the United States being the most, accounting for seven-tenths of the total. Japan, Taiwan, and other places accounted for about 500,000 yuan. There are also Siamese honey oranges, etc., that have not been included. As for American watermelons and the jackfruit, bananas, coconuts, lychees, etc. from the South Seas Islands, imports reached more than 4 million yuan. It is now heard that the Ministry of Industry's Bureau of International Trade, in order to reduce import value, plans to statistically analyze the country's fruit in the shortest time and send personnel to various producing areas to provide guidance and improvement, so that it can develop outward and revitalize the rural economy.

Qian Industry Decides to Settle Accounts at the End of December This Year - Due to Interest Income Tax - Must Wait for General Meeting to Approve Implementation 128

The settlement period for member banks of the Shanghai Banking Association is implemented at the end of June and the end of December each year. As for the settlement period for member money houses of the Qian Industry Association, it has always been implemented on the day of the major year-end closing of each industry (that is, the end of the old lunar year). Now, because the Ministry of Finance has approved the implementation of the deposit interest income tax from January 1 next year, for convenience, it has been resolved by the 28th Executive Committee meeting of the third session to settle all deposits, etc. at the end of December. The above method will be submitted to the members' general meeting tomorrow for approval, and then a notice will be issued to member money houses to comply.

Changbang Rice Boats Stop Measuring - The Hufu Association Sends Personnel to Persuade to Not Stop Measuring Temporarily - Submits a Petition to the Party and Government to Urgently Ban - To Alleviate the Suffering of the People of Jiangsu - Announces to All Sectors - Exposes the Inside Story - Strict Sanctions 131

Zhang Xiehe and others of the Caohujia Du Rice Shop in West Shanghai used heavy measures to retain rice, and because the Changbang Rice Boat Merchants could not bear their exploitation, they decided to implement a measurement stoppage. In order to maintain the food supply for the people of Shanghai, the Changshu Gongsuo in Shanghai held an emergency meeting yesterday, sent personnel to persuade the boat merchants, and submitted a petition to the party and government agencies requesting a ban. The following is an investigation of the situation:

Send Personnel to Persuade

The Changshu Gongsuo in Shanghai, learning that the Changbang Rice Boats in the Caojiadu area were implementing a measurement stoppage in protest against heavy measures to retain rice, held an emergency meeting at 3 pm yesterday at No. 2 Changchunfang, Changan Road, Xinzha Bridge, fearing that it would affect the food supply for the people of Shanghai. More than ten people, including directors Shi Zufuu, Qu Renzhi, Shen Xiaowu, Lu Junwen, Zhu Fusong, Yan Genjin, were present. Chairman Lu Muqin reported that the Caojiadu boat merchants requested a ban on heavy measures to retain rice and were forced to implement a measurement stoppage to strive for it. It was resolved on the spot that, in order to maintain the food supply and regulate grain transportation, Chen Yushu and Xu Yangjian were specially sent to persuade the boat merchants to not stop measuring temporarily, and to wait patiently for the party and government agencies to ban according to law.

Announce to All Sectors

For the purpose of notification, the member boat merchants parked at Caojiadu have reported successively that the shops have instigated the hufu to use heavy measures to retain rice, exploiting profits, and requesting a ban, etc. After the institute received the reports, it sent personnel to negotiate with the shops there, but not only did they not improve, but they also stated that it was a habit of the Caojiadu Rice Shop and difficult to eliminate. We have investigated that our boat merchants transport rice, directly for profit and to make a living, and indirectly also to regulate grain, braving wind and rain, enduring cold and heat, and hoping to make a small profit from transporting rice. Who knew that after the shops and the hufu used heavy measures to retain rice, the amount of rice lost per measure was more than one sheng, and on average, for each boat of 150 dan (300 measures), the loss would be about three or four dan. This kind of evil habit is even more severe than the previous yamen officials and checkpoints. If the boat merchants do not accept heavy measures to retain rice, the shop staff will go on board and grab the rice themselves. If they are not satisfied, they will be beaten. The boat merchants' material losses have been endless over the years. In order to relieve the suffering of the boat merchants, based on the request of the members, this institute plans to temporarily stop measuring. This is not an extra request from our boat merchants, and it will affect the food supply for the people of Shanghai. Whose responsibility is it? For this reason, we are revealing our true feelings, hoping that all sectors will understand.

Request a Ban

A document to the Municipal Party Department and the Bureau of Social Affairs states: "Submitting a petition to ban heavy measures to retain rice in order to maintain the livelihood of the boat merchants. We have investigated that the Caojiadu area rice shops collude with the hufu to use heavy measures to retain rice. After the institute submitted a letter to the Municipal Bureau of Weights and Measures and the Bean and Rice Industry Association requesting a ban, it was approved that the Bean and Rice Industry Association replied that it had notified the industry in both the north and south cities to ban heavy measures to retain rice. The institute immediately notified the boat merchants to comply according to the reply from the association, and after consulting with the Shanghai North Transportation Rice Boat Merchants Association and the north city shops, because it was not easy to eliminate heavy measures temporarily, it was changed to temporarily banning the rice retaining first, and considerable results have been achieved. However, the Caojiadu shops, after the institute sent personnel to negotiate, not only did not accept the ban on heavy measures, but also stated that this was a long-standing custom of Caojiadu and difficult to reform (excerpt omitted). Our boat merchants, because their capital is at stake, would rather sacrifice their business and are unwilling to suffer illegal exploitation. They implement freedom of business in order to passively resist. On the one hand, it is also to urge the shops to consider the difficulties of the boat customers and improve. Who knew that the shops would send staff and apprentices to go on board and grab the rice themselves. If they are not satisfied, they will be beaten. Freedom of business cannot be forced on others. This kind of behavior is no different from bandits. The Changbang Boat Merchants in Caojiadu originally planned to stop measuring as soon as possible to alleviate the suffering. At this time when the Sui border is invaded by bandits, in order to maintain local security and the food supply for the people of Shanghai, we still submit a petition to your (Department) (Bureau) to deal with it properly as soon as possible in accordance with legal procedures, so as to ban it as soon as possible, in order to maintain the business of the boat merchants. This is for the public convenience."

Hu Qingyu, Commissioner for Investigating the League of Nations Administrative Organization specially appointed by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, came to Shanghai a few days ago to wait for the ship after being appointed. The investigation period is six months, and I will return to China next spring.

Hangzhou-Yushan Section Track Replacement Loan Agreement Finalized, Shanghai Syndicate to Provide Loan at 1% Annual Interest for Six Years, Czech Loan of Six Million for Materials to Be Finalized 133

The Sin Sin News reports: The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway's Hangzhou-Yushan section is to replace its tracks with heavier ones. A loan of 2.8 million yuan from a Shanghai syndicate has been agreed upon. Furthermore, the Ministry of Railways is in talks with a Czech company for a loan of 28,000 tons of steel rails and materials, valued at 6 million yuan. These negotiations are nearing completion. Work on the track replacement is scheduled to begin in early January next year, aiming for simultaneous completion and traffic opening with the Nanchang-Pingxiang section. The Sin Sin News reporter has obtained the following detailed information:

Track Replacement Loan Agreement Finalized

The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Council has decided to replace the current 35-pound light rails of the Hangzhou-Yushan section with 63-pound heavy rails, aligning it with the Yushan-Nanchang and Nanchang-Pingxiang sections. Besides materials, the required construction cost is 2.8 million yuan. After negotiations with the Shanghai syndicate, consisting of the Bank of China, the Farmers Bank of China, and the Zhejiang Local Bank (the China Industrial and Commercial Bank and Zhejiang Industrial Bank have withdrawn), a draft agreement has been finalized. According to the reporter's inquiries, the agreement includes: (1) The Bank of China will be responsible for 1.8 million yuan, while the Farmers Bank of China and the Zhejiang Local Bank will each handle 500,000 yuan. (2) All assets and business income of the Hangzhou-Yushan section will be used as collateral. (3) The annual interest rate is 1%, with the principal and interest to be fully repaid within six years. Jin Runquan, the representative of the syndicate and the manager of the Bank of China's Hangzhou branch, has telegraphed the head office and plans to personally visit Shanghai soon to further discuss the matter with the head office and the other two banks before formally signing the agreement.

Materials Loan Also Nearing Success

In addition to the construction costs for the Hangzhou-Yushan section's replacement with 63-pound heavy rails, which are being borrowed from the Shanghai syndicate, the steel rails, sleepers, and other materials will be borrowed by the Ministry of Railways from a Czech railway materials factory. The materials include 28,000 tons of steel rails, valued at 6 million yuan in national currency. According to banking circles, the loan is progressing smoothly. After several rounds of negotiations between the two parties, an agreement is generally in sight and is expected to be successfully signed soon. The annual interest rate is expected to be between 4% and 5%, with a term of six years. The contract signing will follow the precedent of the previous Yushan-Nanchang and Nanchang-Pingxiang sections, borrowing materials from the German Otto Wolff steel factory, so there should be no problems.

Track Replacement Scheduled to Begin

The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau has been ordered to complete the Nanchang-Pingxiang section by the end of March next year. All construction loans have been negotiated with the syndicate, and the amount of disbursements has been increased since this month, so the progress of various projects is quite rapid. It is expected to be completed before the deadline in March next year. It has been decided to advance the start of the Hangzhou-Yushan section track replacement project to early January next year. Before all materials arrive, materials from the Nanchang-Pingxiang section will be temporarily borrowed, aiming for simultaneous completion with the Nanchang-Pingxiang section. At that time, the entire route of the Hangzhou-Yushan, Yushan-Nanchang, and Nanchang-Pingxiang sections will be fully open to traffic to facilitate transportation. Whether it can be realized according to the planned method depends on the progress of the project.

Revised Long-Distance Telephone Business Regulations to Be Implemented Today, Shanghai Telephone Bureau Notifies Users Yesterday 134

The Ministry of Communications has revised the domestic long-distance telephone business regulations, which will be implemented simultaneously across the country starting today. The Shanghai Telephone Bureau issued a special notice to its users yesterday, stating: "We have received Instruction No. 4025 of the Ministry of Communications' Electrical Affairs Department, which states: 'After examination, the number of long-distance telephone lines in various regions of the country has expanded year by year. The long-distance telephone lines of nine provinces have also been opened for business one after another. The Shanghai-Hankou wireless telephone has also been opened for communication. Long-distance telephone business is becoming increasingly complex. The long-distance telephone business regulations promulgated by the Ministry on June 2, 1933, are no longer suitable for the current business situation. Therefore, new domestic long-distance telephone business regulations have been formulated, which were promulgated on October 15 of this year and stipulated to take effect from December 1. Now, we are sending you 50 copies each of the domestic long-distance telephone business regulations and the domestic long-distance telephone classification price comparison table. Please comply with them and instruct others to comply with them.' Therefore, we should comply with it and implement it from tomorrow (i.e., today). In addition to printing the domestic long-distance telephone business regulations and the classification price comparison table in the first half of the 26th year telephone directory of this bureau for distribution to users and for reference, the important provisions of the new regulations are listed as follows: (1) Changes in the names of various types of calls. Previously, it was called 'Ordinary Call,' now it is changed to 'Normal Call.' 'Expedited Call' is now changed to 'Expedited Call.' 'Ordinary Notification' is changed to 'Normal Caller.' 'Expedited Notification' is changed to 'Expedited Caller.' 'Ordinary Call' is changed to 'Normal Call.' 'Expedited Call' remains 'Expedited Call.' 'Scheduled Call' is changed to 'Timed Call.' (2) Changes in the scope of calls. The current regulations stipulate that the scope of calls is limited to three kilometers from the bureau, a reduction of two kilometers compared to the past. (3) Changes in the call fee. Article 17 of the new regulations stipulates that the price of a call is the same as the price of a caller, and the previously charged special effort fee has been canceled. The above three points are the most important differences compared to the past. As for the special business chapter in the new regulations, all special calls and timed calls will be suspended until detailed measures are formulated. The night calls will still be handled in accordance with the previous regulations. Furthermore, the prices of all calls are based on the normal call prices specified in the ordinary price list. You can find out by referring to the classification price comparison table. Note: 1. All prices are based on national currency. 2. The prices specified in the ordinary price list are the normal call prices. If you want to know the normal caller, normal call, expedited call, expedited caller, or expedited call price from a certain place to a certain place, you should first check the normal call price between the two places in the ordinary price list, and then use the normal call price as a basis for comparison with this table to get the price you want to know. For example, the normal call price between Nanjing and Hankou is 2 yuan, then the normal caller price is 2.4 yuan, the expedited caller price is 4.4 yuan, and so on. 3. The cancellation fee from a certain place to a certain place is the same for all types of calls. 4. The call fee and cancellation fee for all types of telephone calls between Zhejiang Province are calculated and charged separately according to the ministry line and the provincial line, regardless of whether it is a caller or a call, and regardless of whether it is normal or expedited. The above is only a summary. If users need the 'Ministry of Communications Domestic Long-Distance Telephone Business Regulations,' they can obtain it from the business section of the bureau."

China Merchants Inland River Bureau to Close by the End of the Year 137

19 Small Steamers Sold to Repay Debts The closure of the China Merchants Inland River Steamship Bureau, as ordered by the Ministry of Communications, has been reported in the newspapers. According to a report from the Datong News Agency, the bureau has been delayed in closing due to existing lease contracts for its small steamers on various inland river routes. However, in order to comply with the ministry's order, the bureau has decided to expedite the closure by the end of this month (i.e., the end of the year). Navigation will be suspended from January 1st next year. All 19 small steamers will be sold to repay debts.

Large Quantities of Rice Transported to Shanghai from Rice-Producing Areas 139

Very Little Rice Confiscated in Qingpu and Other Counties After rice was confiscated in Qingpu, Jinshan, Xinghua, and other counties when it was being transported out of the area, the rice industry in Shanghai, believing that this violated the central government's public order on rice circulation regulation, requested the authorities of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to order the counties that had confiscated the rice to release it quickly. According to rice industry sources, the amount of rice confiscated in these counties is small. Other rice-producing areas can still transport rice to Shanghai, so there is no impact on the city's food supply and rice market. Moreover, since the Shanghai rice industry appealed to the authorities of the two provinces, the rice is expected to be released within a few days, and similar incidents should not occur again in the future.

QINGYUN JEWELRY STORE EMPLOYEE STEALS GOLD JEWELRY AND LEGAL TENDER WORTH OVER 20,000 YUAN, ALSO SETS FIRE TO DESTROY EVIDENCE, POLICE REQUEST SEVERE PUNISHMENT 141

Wu Zuyao, a 25-year-old native of Ningbo, has been working as an apprentice and later promoted to warehouse keeper at Qingyun Jewelry Store at No. 685 Nanjing Road for ten years. This summer, due to a debt of over 700 yuan owed to the store, he was dismissed by the manager, Yan Zhijun. Wu then resided at No. 201 Chongqing Road. Because he was familiar with all the store's employees, he still frequented the store. At about 8 p.m. on the 26th of the month, after Qingyun had closed, Wu went there again to chat with the store staff.

Since Wu had worked in the store for quite some time, he was very familiar with the location of the important keys. Taking advantage of everyone's inattention, he stole the safe key kept by Zhuang Yingxia, the silver box key kept by Liu Shutang, and the gold jewelry box key kept by Wu Xinpei. He then stole 122 taels of gold jewelry (worth 16,800 yuan) and 4868 yuan in legal tender, put them in a rattan box, and hired a

Southern Motor Vehicle

to go home. Before leaving, in an attempt to destroy the evidence, he set fire to the paper wrapping the gold jewelry, intending to set the fire to destroy the evidence. Although the fire started at the time, it only charred part of the wall panel and the box. The fire was extinguished immediately, and no major disaster occurred. The next morning, Zhuang Yingxia discovered the theft and reported it to the manager, who then reported it to the Old Gate Patrol Room. Chief Detective Lu Gengsheng and Detective Song Wenqing and Zhu Heshang were immediately ordered to investigate and found that Wu was suspected of

Major Suspicion

They immediately went to Wu's relatives to investigate Wu's whereabouts. After stealing the gold jewelry and banknotes, Wu initially hid them at his residence, but thinking it was not safe, he moved all the stolen goods to his wife's brother, Ye Xinde, at Yuanhe Herbal Medicine Shop, No. 119 Lizhou Gua Street, Nanshi, on the same night, intending to retrieve them the next day. However, the police had already found out and Ye handed over all the stolen goods deposited by Wu. Only

Less Than Legal Tender

Fifty-two yuan were missing, and the rest were complete. Wu did come the next day and was immediately apprehended by the detectives. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the First Criminal Division of the Special First Court. The patrol room lawyer, Ru Baoyi, explained the case and filed a public prosecution in accordance with Articles 321(1) and 321(2) and Article 173(3) of the Criminal Law. He also stated that according to the patrol room's investigation, Qingyun Jewelry Store has 30 silversmiths, 25 employees, and 5 coolies, living on the second and third floors of the store. The vault is downstairs. If the

Fire Had Been Caused

The lives of 60 people would have been lost. Therefore, the defendant's crime is heinous and should be severely punished according to law. When questioned, Wu Zuyao pleaded guilty. After reviewing the confession, Criminal Judge Qian Hongye announced the judgment in court. Wu Zuyao was sentenced to three years and six months in prison for attempting to set fire to a building where people were present. The stolen goods were returned to the original owner.

The Bao Gang Case Continued Yesterday, Witnesses Called Testified Inconsistently With Court Order, Continued Hearing Awaited 142

Lawyer Bao Gang and Cui Changgui, bodyguard of Liu Huaizhi, captain of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Detective Team, are accused of seducing Yang Yuehua, Cui's cohabitating fiancée, and Zhang Qinghong, the third district chief of Chuansha County, of harboring Bao Gang's teahouse worker Zhang Xinkui, thereby aiding in the seduction. The local court's prosecutor has publicly prosecuted Bao Gang and Zhang Xinkui for violating family ethics, and the Jiangsu Surveillance Commissioner's Office has also dispatched personnel to investigate and report Zhang Qinghong. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, this case was again heard in Criminal Court One by Judge Xie Zhengnong. Bao Gang testified that he was 34 years old, from Nanhui, and a graduate of the law program at Chizhi College. He did not know Zhang Qinghong and was not classmates with him. Yang Yuehua came to his house at 3:00 PM on May 10th, saying that Cui Changgui often abused her and requested legal representation. He advised that since they had cohabitated for two or three years, there was no need to go to extremes, and he would write a letter to warn him to reconcile. Yang Yuehua signed her name herself, and he did not take her to the Da Fang Hotel. On May 17th, he was in a meeting at the Pingshe ticket office at 640 Avenue Edward VII until 10:00 PM, so the alleged seduction trip to Chuansha on the 17th was inconsistent timewise. He also said that Zhang Qinghong and his wife were colluding to frame him. Then, Zhang Xinkui testified that he was 48 years old, from Nanhui, and worked as a teahouse worker for Bao Gang. On May 10th, Yang Yuehua came to Bao's house, saying she wanted to find Lawyer Bao to file a lawsuit. He led her to the door of his office, where a guest was walking out, and the door was not closed, but ajar. Yang Yuehua went in herself. The next morning at 8:00 AM, he went out to buy porridge and side dishes. Yang Yuehua asked him if Lawyer Bao was awake, and he said no. After eating breakfast at home, he went to the countryside, telling the rickshaw driver "A'er" to do so, and then he left. It was because his niece was getting married, and he was bringing a pillow core and dried bamboo shoots to the countryside from Shanghai. However, his niece had already come to Shanghai to her brother's house, and her brother was giving her away. Three days after his niece's wedding, he went to his nephew's place in Shanghai, and his niece and her husband came back to their maiden home. He met his nephew-in-law once, and then returned to the countryside for the seventh-day memorial service for his mother. He had not returned to Bao Gang's place, and this was his alibi, etc. At this point, Bao Gang's defense lawyer said that Yang Yuehua had previously testified that when she had intercourse with Bao, she felt that Bao had gonorrhea. He requested that the new forensic report be reviewed. The judge said that it had not yet been returned. Zhang's niece was then called. Miss Zhang testified that she was 23 years old, from Beicai Town, Nanhui. Zhang Xinkui was her paternal uncle, and her husband was named Gu Fengzhou, who lived at 14 Gujiazhai, Shanghai. She was married on the 26th day of the leap month in the lunar calendar this year, which was when she came to Shanghai, and her uncle arrived in the countryside on the 21st. She had seen him. The second day after the wedding, she returned to her maiden home at her brother's house on Fuxing Road in the French Concession, and her uncle was also at her brother's place in Shanghai, etc. At this point, Gu Fengzhou was questioned and testified that he was 35 years old, and Miss Gu-Zhang was his wife. They were married on the 26th day of the third month, and she returned to her maiden home that day. He had already met Zhang Xinkui and exchanged greetings, and on the 27th, a sedan chair came to pick up him and his wife, and they also ate at the same table. The judge immediately ordered the three to come to the court to be questioned as to why their testimonies did not match, and they all stammered. At this point, Mrs. Zhang Yao testified that she was 23 years old, from Chuansha. Zhang Qinghong was her husband and had not come today. The judge instructed that he must be brought to the court next time. Mrs. Zhang said, "Yes." Yang Yuehua was also asked if she knew Bao Gang, and she replied that she did not know him at first. Bao was a classmate of her husband from Chizhi University and came often. Around May 20th, Bao brought Yang Yuehua, saying that she was his concubine and was staying for a few days because she was not getting along with his wife. It lasted for two weeks. Bao came once in the first week, and the two of them closed the back room. Later, Yang Yuehua went to Shanghai and came back three days later, where Cui Changgui found her. The Yangtze River Rises Again, and River Transportation Is Smooth 148

The water level of the Yangtze River has been very shallow. The Jiujiang-Hankou section had dropped to 9 feet 1 inch at its lowest point. Later, the Jianghan Customs surveying vessel discovered a new channel of 10 feet 3 inches, and river steamers were able to resume traffic. However, the navigable section of the new channel was too narrow, and only single steamers could navigate, so river steamers traveling to and fro in the new channel still felt inconvenience. The shallowest point upstream was near Xinzhou and Daijiazhou near Huangshigang above Jiujiang. The various river steamers that were blocked from passing were also in these two places. The Madang area also prohibited night navigation from the 26th. The Sixth Company's ships with shallower drafts could barely pass through the shallow water section, but the cargo loaded on the upstream and downstream steamers was reduced. Today, increased shallow water fees are being implemented. However, yesterday, various steamship companies in Shanghai suddenly received a telegram from Hankou stating that the water level in the Jiujiang-Hankou section had suddenly risen, from 9 feet 1 inch to 10 feet 8 inches, and then from 10 feet 8 inches to 12 feet, and that the Xun-Han section could be safely navigated. The companies were overjoyed and, starting today, ordered the Yangtze River steamers to load more cargo and be able to go directly to Hankou without having to unload at Jiujiang. There are reportedly two reasons for the rise in water level: (1) the weather is warming up; (2) the riverbed is gradually deepening after the shallow water area has been navigated up and down by various river steamers with great difficulty for many days.

The Telegraph Bureau Will Pilot a Method of Returning Telegram Receipts, Starting Today 153

In order to make it easier for people sending telegrams to obtain receipts from the recipients, the Ministry of Communications has specially formulated the "Provisional Measures for the Telegraph Bureau to Return Telegram Receipts," which will be piloted starting December 1st. According to the measures, the sender only needs to pay an additional nine cents for postage, including the postage for single registered printed matter, and indicate the word "receipt" in the telegraph header (RRCP in English telegraphs). The receiving bureau will then issue a "receipt" signed by the recipient and send it to the sending bureau for the sender to keep for verification. At the receiving bureau, an extra copy of the receipt should be prepared for incoming telegrams requiring receipts, and the recipient should be asked to sign and stamp it. Therefore, in reality, the recipient who receives a telegram needs to stamp two receipts. The first one is the receipt from the receiving bureau, which is the receipt on the telegram envelope, and the other one is the "telegram receipt received," which is prepared to be sent to the sender. The above-mentioned method of returning receipts is also applicable to distributed telegrams (that is, one telegram is sent to several recipients), and only one cent of postage is required. However, the word "receipt" must be written before the address and name of each recipient, for example, "Distributed by so-and-so for two receipts - No. so-and-so, so-and-so Street, Nanjing - receipt, so-and-so, so-and-so Street." In addition, if the sender sends multiple telegrams to the same city at the same time, and all of them need to use the receipt method, only one postage fee will be charged. If they are not sent at the same time, the postage fee cannot be reduced. This receipt method is especially suitable for telegrams with monetary relations and other urgent telegrams, or social telegrams with gift certificates attached. However, it is not applicable to international telegrams and domestic news, weather, shipping, and relief telegrams. It is reported that the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau of this port has started preparations after receiving the ministry's order and will implement it as scheduled, and has distributed the methods and other information to all sectors for reference.

Sudden Cold Weather Causes Typhoid Fever to Run Rampant, 58 Patients Last Week, 16 Deaths 154

Recently, the weather has been cloudy and the weather has suddenly turned cold. People with weak bodies are susceptible to typhoid fever, and it spreads very quickly. The Yong Heng Is Damaged The Yong Heng ship of the Yong An Shipping Company, weighing 1,196 tons, arrived at Yangjiadu Pier in Pudong on the 28th of this month and unloaded its cargo. It was intended to set sail immediately. However, when leaving the pier, the ship's engine blade and axle were entangled by an iron wire cable on the pier, causing the engine to lose all power. The ship could not sail. The company urgently hired water ghosts to enter the river bottom to investigate and find a way to remove the tangled cable. The work lasted all day, but it still could not be completed by night. The water ghosts went ashore and said that there was no way to remove the cable wrapped around the blade and shaft. The company had no choice but to agree with the Jiangnan Shipyard yesterday to tow the Yong Heng into the shipyard by barge, so that technicians could find a way to remove the tangled cable and repair the engine blade and inspect the shaft for damage. The direct and indirect losses have been extremely heavy.

Dockside Boat Damaged 163

The Sanbei Company's "Awakened Lion" steamship, arriving in Shanghai on the morning of the day before yesterday at eight o'clock, was sailing past the Pudong Lujiazui outer Bund area when a local resident, Chen Jingtang's, No. 56567 dockside boat, loaded with 350 bales of cottonseed and sailing from the south, caught sight of the "Awakened Lion." The boat hurriedly turned its rudder to divert towards the Puxi side to avoid collision. However, due to the rapid ebb tide, the boat's hull drifted north quickly. The "Awakened Lion" could not stop in time and violently collided with the right bow of Chen's boat. The boat, being made of wood, immediately broke apart, took on water, and sank. Customs water police, upon receiving the alert, urgently dispatched officers aboard a small steamer to provide assistance, ordering nearby boatmen to first retrieve the soaked cotton seeds from the sunken boat's hold and place them on their boats to reduce the weight of the sunken boat and prevent it from sinking into the bottom of the river. They then towed the empty hull to the Bund, where they beached it. All the salvaged wet cotton seeds were loaded onto another empty boat to await further investigation. It is reported that the owner of the goods is Hengxingtai of Caojiadu. Mrs. Fei Meide, President of the American Women's Association, followed with a speech, stating that today's China has made great progress in all aspects, which is a sign of the revival of the nation and a bright future. She deeply feels the importance of the child welfare cause, so she has forgotten that she is a Westerner and is willing to do her best to follow in the footsteps of the gentlemen and work together towards the goal of child welfare. She believes that the general enlightened people of your country will surely actively join this great child welfare movement in order to consolidate the foundation of the country and strive to stand tall in the world. The guests and hosts exchanged opinions and had a very pleasant time. The meeting adjourned at around 1 PM.

Ye Fokang Reconciles with Wang Hanqing; Wang Disappears; Court Summons Witness Tomorrow 168

Lawyer Ye Fokang was impeached by Attorney Tang Ruxiu of the Shanghai District Court Prosecutor's Office for embezzling a huge amount of money from Wang Hanqing during litigation. It was originally scheduled to be questioned yesterday, but Wang Hanqing had already reached a reconciliation with Ye, so Wang disappeared, and the indictment and summons could not be delivered. The court bailiff has reported the case as closed. The court has now decided to have Judge Lu Hongyi question the case on the afternoon of December 2nd and summon witnesses such as lawyers Fan Gang, Gu Ao, Zha Renwei, Gu Darong, and others.

Shanghai Municipal Council Explains Issue of Collecting Empty House Tax; Responds to United Citizens' Association 169

Since the January 28th Incident in Shanghai, various industries have been sluggish and unable to maintain operations. The reason is that housing is too expensive and unbearable. The Chinese Residents Association of the Public Concession and the United Citizens' Association of the First Special District believe that the French Concession has implemented the collection of empty house taxes, which is sufficient to reduce rents. Therefore, they successively suggested that the Shanghai Municipal Council follow suit to seek the revival of the market. After receiving the letter, the Shanghai Municipal Council replied to the United Citizens' Association of the First Special District yesterday, stating: "We acknowledge your letter of November 20th regarding the collection of empty house taxes in the French Concession. We believe that your association has some misunderstandings about this matter. According to our information, if vacant houses in the French Concession that are for rent have furniture and equipment, half of the tax will be waived. Vacant houses without such equipment are not subject to tax. Within the Public Concession, vacant houses with such equipment are still subject to the full tax. This is our response."

Overseas Chinese Petition Representatives from the Philippines, Liang Cikuang and Others, Travel to Beijing 170

Liang Cikuang and Cen Xinyi, representatives of overseas Chinese returning to China from the Philippines to petition, reported to the local Overseas Chinese Affairs authorities on Monday after arriving in Shanghai the day before yesterday. Although the British Embassy in China has not yet been able to formally move from Peiping to Nanjing, it has established a branch office in Nanjing. Recent News from the Chinese Company of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps 173

Recruitment Preparation

The Chinese Company of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps recruits reserve members once a year to provide training and replenishment. Merchants in the city who are interested in joining in order to acquire military knowledge and serve the public can obtain an application form at the Chinese Company Headquarters at No. 131 Hankou Road and register.

Encampment of Translators

The various companies of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps hold encampments every year in order to carry out intensive training in accordance with regulations. It is learned that the encampment course for members of the Chinese Company this year has already been completed. The translators' corps is scheduled to hold it at the Hongkou shooting range barracks on the 12th and 13th of this month. It is said that the two corps will jointly hold an awards ceremony on the afternoon of the 13th and invite members' families and guests to visit. It is expected that there will be a lively scene at that time.

Promotion of Officers

The corps recently received Order No. 46 from headquarters, which stated that, according to a Shanghai Municipal Council gazette, Sergeants Xu Shaomei, Xia Zaiyu, Zhong Yuting, and three other members of the Translators' Corps have been promoted to the rank of Second Lieutenant as of the current date. Order No. 45 also announced that Sergeant Wu Shouwen has been promoted to Quartermaster of the Translators' Corps. Mr. Xia has also held an important position in the Junpei Bureau for many years. Mr. Zhong is the manager of Lulin Foreign Company. Mr. Wu Shouwen is currently a representative of Watson's Company. These gentlemen are all outstanding talents in the Chinese Company.

Long Service Medal

According to the regulations of the Shanghai Volunteer Corps, those who have served for twelve years and are competent will be awarded a long service medal by the Shanghai Municipal Council. Those who continue to serve for five years will receive one star, and those who serve for ten years will receive two stars as commendation. It is learned that the Chinese Company members who have received the long service medal this year include the Medical Officer Niu Huilin, as well as Bao Xianqiang, Xie Hong, Wei Qi, Zhang Naibin, Wang Zexiang, He Bingcheng, Huang Jusheng, Zhu Gengxin, Cao Shengzhang, and ten other members. Captain Chen Shixia, Sheng Shaoming, and Wang Weishan have received one star. Song Yunqi and Liu Jinghe have received three stars. It is said that both gentlemen have been in the corps for 27 years, so they have received this high honor. Their enthusiasm and perseverance are truly commendable.

The Shanghai County government has convened a meeting to decide on the prevention and control of rice stem borers this year. It has also been scheduled that the county government, county party headquarters, Third District Office, and Beiqiao District Branch will hold a publicity conference and lecture meeting in Beiqiao Town on December 5th. Yang Weiquan's Famous Work "Jin Huidui" Comes Out 176

Yang Weiquan, a recluse from ancient Fujian, is a famous modern painter and calligrapher. His work "Jin Huidui" is ingeniously designed, unique, lively in brush and ink, and reminiscent of the ancients. Its exquisite and unparalleled aspects, along with Qian Shunju's "Jin Huidui" of the Song Dynasty, shine together, before and after. Famous figures such as Yu Youren, Wang Zhengting, and Guang Fan have all praised it and set its price, making it clear that it is valuable. It is said that the price is ten yuan per foot, and ten yuan per piece for album pages and fan surfaces. Payment is required before the ink is applied, and an additional 10% ink fee is charged. For communication and contact, one can go directly to Yang's residence at No. 142 Huajin Archway in the city, or inquire at the Xinbao newspaper office, which can also assist in the contact.

Huang Lansun's Encoffining Held Yesterday; Coffin Temporarily Placed in the Huining Association Hall 177

Mr. Huang Lansun of Xiuning passed away on November 28th due to illness. His body was encoffined at the Chinese Funeral Home on Haig Road yesterday morning. China Economic Yearbook Published 178

The Sino-Foreign Publishing House at No. 230 Route Pichon has, in light of the fact that our national government is now striving to promote the National Economic Construction Movement, recognized the urgent need for detailed surveys and accurate statistics on the organization and status of the economy throughout the country in order to base improvements on facts and use them as guidelines for facilities. Therefore, it has specially compiled and printed the China Economic Yearbook for reference by all sectors and to benefit experts in their research. The entire book is a hardcover volume with content divided into ten major sectors: agriculture, mining, industry, commerce, foreign trade, finance, fiscal affairs, transportation, labor, and overseas Chinese economy. It contains more than 300,000 words and is fresh in its material and rich in its collection. The foreword includes prefaces by financial giants Yu Zuoting and Wang Xiaolai, and economic experts Zhu Xinong and others. The hardcover price is two yuan per copy, and the paperback price is one yuan and five jiao. It is currently sold by the Shanghai Magazine Company at No. 324 Fourth Road. Homicide with Ax in Jiaheli; Hua Shihao Dies; Murderer Yang Hanzhang Still Tries to Evade Responsibility, Claiming It Was Caused by Resistance to Attack 181

Hua Shihao, courtesy name Zhaokun, a native of Hubei residing at No. 51 Jiaheli, Lane 81, Hedder Road, was a boxing instructor at the National Martial Arts Hall in Jiujiang County. No. 46 in the same lane is the clubhouse of the Hubei Native Place Association, so Hua often went there to play. Due to gambling issues, he had a feud with Yang Hanzhang, a native of Hubei living in the Native Place Association, and they were incompatible. On the night of the 21st of this month, Yang hid two axes and ambushed Hua Shihao at the entrance of Jiaheli Lane. When Hua Shihao arrived, he drew the axe and struck Hua's head several times, causing Hua to fall to the ground with injuries. Yang fled with the axe to the intersection of Foch Road and Haig Road, where he was arrested by Indian Constable No. 311 along with the murder weapon. They were taken to the Jing'an Temple Police Station, and Hua Shihao was sent to Renji Hospital. Due to the severity of his injuries, he died despite medical treatment. Yang Hanzhang was escorted to the First Special Court for interrogation and custody. Yesterday morning, Judge Chuan Lin came to the Eighth Criminal Court to continue the interrogation. According to police attorney Wang Yaotang, he was charged with murder under Article 271 of the Criminal Law. When questioned, the defendant Yang Hanzhang confessed that he had no feud with the deceased Hua Shihao, but he and Zhang Dongshan and Zhang Yunshan had disagreements over collecting commissions for gambling. Zhang and others then asked Hua Shihao for help, and Hua became deeply hostile to him, using his strength to intimidate him, causing him to not dare to go to the Native Place Association to stay for several days. On the night of the 21st of this month, he carried an axe, intending to return to the association. Unexpectedly, he met Hua Shihao in the lane. Hua immediately drew a nine-section whip and said, "Good fellow, you've come?" After speaking, he struck at him. He then met the attack with the axe. The nine-section whip wrapped around the axe. After he pulled hard, he also used another axe to wound his head. At that time, Zhang Dongshan and others also arrived and made things difficult for him. He had no choice but to escape and report to the Indian constable, and so on. Under the compulsory defense of lawyer Fan Gang assigned by the court, the defendant was ordered to be remanded in custody pending judgment next Monday.

Weather Report 191

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: Shandong Province and the Yellow River basin are cloudy with sand and strong northwesterly winds. The middle and upper reaches of the Yangtze River are changing from cloudy to overcast, with rain in several locations and variable winds. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River are cloudy with smog or sand and whirlwinds due to a small low-pressure system moving northeast. The East China Sea is cloudy with strong southeasterly to southwesterly winds. Taiwan has northeasterly winds. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in Shanghai was 69.4 degrees, and the lowest was 45.9 degrees. The highest and lowest temperatures on the same day last year were 63.1 and 52.7 degrees, respectively.

China Sports Federation Women's Basketball - Opens Today - Patriotic vs. Qixiu - Held at Qixiu 196

The China School Sports Federation Women's Basketball Championship is scheduled to begin today. Only three schools are participating: Patriotic, Qixiu, and Chongde. Shanghai Boy Scouts - Actively Forming Wartime Service Corps - Qualifications for Corps Members Have Been Drafted 201

The Shanghai Boy Scouts organized a battlefield service corps during the "January 28th" Shanghai battle to rescue wounded soldiers and refugees. Their spirit and perseverance were admired by the people of the country. Now, when the border bandits are creating chaos and the war in Suiyuan is tense, the people of the country are rising up to help the soldiers fighting the bandits. According to him, in addition to promoting the One-Day Movement, the Shanghai Boy Scouts are actively organizing a wartime service corps in order to be ready to go out and serve. The age and skills of all the Boy Scouts in the city have been investigated and are about to be completed. All the Boy Scouts have now been notified to register voluntarily. The qualifications for participation are provisionally set as follows: (1) All Shanghai Boy Scouts who are 15 years of age or older and have more than one year of Boy Scout experience; (2) Those who are in good health and have been certified by a doctor; (3) Those who must fill out a volunteer form and have the consent of their parents; (4) Those who must absolutely obey orders during the service period and are willing to be severely punished for any violations of laws and regulations; (5) Those who register must have a written guarantee from the principal or leader.

Middle School Principals' Association Issues Declaration of Establishment 203

The Shanghai Middle School Principals' Association was officially established the day before yesterday. Yesterday, the association issued the following declaration of establishment: In the face of intensifying international conflicts and the exchange of Chinese national revival movements, the position of the education community is becoming increasingly important, and the responsibilities it bears are also becoming increasingly heavy. We should respond to the needs of the times and seek fundamental reforms in the education undertaking. Thus, this association has been established. After the establishment, how to make education practice have a positive expression, how to make the direction of young people's lives have serious and reasonable guidance, how to make the education undertaking have a close connection with society and the country, and become a vibrant and brilliant education, the future facts can answer. Now, we will reveal the four points that this association plans to strive for to inform the people of the country:

We need national culture (1) Since Chairman Chiang Kai-shek advocated the New Life Movement, some people have advocated the Chinese-based cultural construction movement. The premise of the two is what is called "not adhering to the old" and "not blindly following." But what exactly is Chinese-based culture has not yet been concluded. We believe that culture is the general expression of a country's people striving for survival. What China should strive for now is, of course, the economic construction of the Three Principles of the People, but to achieve this goal, there must be two prerequisites: the invasion of imperialism is internal, namely, the loss of national spirit. Therefore, the essence of the culture that China needs, although economic, its starting point is nationalism. The education undertaking is a part of cultural construction. It bears the task of pioneering, cultivating the foundation, and deepening the source in the overall system of national culture. It should undoubtedly stand on the basis of nationalism, temper the fighting spirit of young people, and give play to the inherent ability of the nation. Externally, we should seek the freedom and equality of the country. Internally, we should seek the regeneration and development of the national economy. This is the first point we need to strive for. We should cultivate national defense education (2) The quality of education depends on whether it can meet the needs of reality. The Chinese national revival movement should, of course, be considered from a long-term perspective, but the situation of the confrontation between the two fronts of peace and aggression has become sharp and expanded. The total outbreak of the world crisis is imminent. China is under the dual pressure of the political and military forces of strong enemies. The life of the nation and the peace of the Far East are in danger. In fact, it is no longer a time to calmly build and talk and laugh to retreat from the enemy. In recent years, the government has made great determination for national defense construction and has made significant achievements. However, this responsibility must be borne jointly by the government and the people. The education community is responsible and cannot shirk it. Therefore, the current stage of school education should cultivate spiritual national defense in the field of social sciences, and in the field of natural sciences, it should, according to its nature, do its best to engage in the research and production of national defense preparations. In terms of management and training, it should be absolutely militarized. Not only should it develop the habits of hard work, endurance, meticulousness, and speed, but also pay attention to the exercises of combat, rescue, intelligence, propaganda, poison prevention, and air defense at all times. Even a question or a competition must contain the meaning of national defense. This is the second point we need to strive for. Integrate education with life (3) Education and life are mutually causal, that is, one has to receive education for the sake of life, and only the promotion of education can make social life continuously improve and move forward. Leaving life, except for a part of outstanding young people who can adapt to social life, the rest not only have no entrepreneurial ability, but also face obstacles everywhere in employment. Thus, a large number of graduating young people are trapped in an atmosphere of unemployment and hunger and cannot extricate themselves. This phenomenon, of course, has economic and political reasons, and the implementation of education and the late festival of social life are not one of the reasons. In recent years, vocational education has been put into practice from theory, but most middle schools have not changed their course. In schools of vocational education, although the disciplines have gradually approached the profession, in fact, they are still not linked to vocational institutions, and vocational institutions do not seem to attach importance to vocational education. As for the daily life of students, it is even more isolated from society and lacks general social experience and knowledge. This is the third point we need to strive for.

Lead the education community in the aid-Suiyuan movement (4) The importance of Suiyuan in national defense is clear to everyone. If Suiyuan is lost, the provinces of North China cannot be guaranteed, and even the entire China is in danger of becoming a colony. On the enemy's side, in order to complete its established policy of encircling Outer Mongolia and invading North China, it is determined to seize Suiyuan. The government has launched a national liberation war to protect national survival and territorial integrity. Tens of thousands of loyal soldiers of the country have fought bloody battles on the snowy front and have shown their power, repeatedly defeating strong enemies and capturing Bailingmiao, the base of the bandits. Now, the people of the whole country have risen up to respond, saving on food and clothing to contribute to the front line. The development of public sentiment and the strength of the military force are all symbols of national revival. The education community is in the leading position of young people, and it should use all its talents and resources to advocate for it. This is the fourth point we need to strive for. The above four points are all efforts that this association should make in the future. We will not shirk our responsibility and will certainly achieve our goals. We vow to move forward with the great fearless spirit of Premier Sun and the hard-working creed shown by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. We hope that the education authorities and people from all walks of life will give us guidance and supervision so as to increase our effectiveness. We are very fortunate.

American Philosopher, Mr. Alexander, Sympathizes with Chinese Culture 204

Mr. Hartlay B. Alexander, a professor at the Claremont Graduate University of Southern California, and a world-renowned philosopher, lectured on "National Culture and World Civilization" at Zhejiang University in Hangzhou. He is a former president of the American Philosophical Association and a director of the Southwestern Archaeological Society of America. He has also lectured at the University of Paris and has a wide range of academic interests. He initially worked as an editor for the Webster's Dictionary, and also authored two large volumes on North and South American mythology, as well as several volumes of poetry and drama. He has also written numerous commentaries on education, literary construction, and political philosophy. Additionally, he served as an editor for the "Encyclopedia of Philosophy" and the "World Book Encyclopedia". However, the core of his thinking is rooted in the ancient Greek philosopher Plato, and his sympathy for Chinese culture is based on this foundation. This year, at the age of sixty-three, he is energetic and shows no signs of aging. During his travels, he visited President Zhu Kezhen of National Zhejiang University in Hangzhou, as well as Mr. Mei Kedi, the head of the university's foreign language department, who invited him to give a lecture. Mr. Alexander then delivered a lecture at Zhejiang University on the 21st of this month, titled "National Culture and World Civilization," which included the following points: (1) China today needs modern science and mechanical construction, but it must be understood that the entirety of human life is more than just machinery. Mechanical life is only a part of human civilization. Westerners only know this partial aspect and cannot see the whole picture. In this regard, the wisdom of the Chinese people far surpasses that of Europeans and Americans, because Chinese people can pursue a complete human life encompassing truth, beauty, and goodness. (2) Any national culture is an expression of the creative life of the entire nation, each possessing unique and indelible value. Therefore, for the sake of the nation itself and for world civilization, each nation should always maintain and promote the unique characteristics of its inherent culture without losing them. Looking at the beautiful mountains and clear waters of West Lake, I am even more convinced of the greatness of this national creative power. If you continue to work hard, the world will benefit. (3) Monotony and uniformity kill vitality, whether for individuals or nations. What is valuable is mutual respect and mutual understanding, not necessarily becoming identical. Today's international misfortune stems from a lack of understanding. For example, Americans often misunderstand China, and at the same time, Chinese people also misunderstand America. To seek the welfare of the world, China and the United States must each maintain and promote their national strengths, respecting and befriending each other, just as each individual develops their talents and strengths without everyone needing to follow the same path. World civilization must be composed of the different and unique cultures of each nation. I hope that Chinese people who bear cultural responsibility will encourage each other to strive for this goal.

Ministry of Education Urges Guangdong Province to Promote National Language Education 205

The Ministry of Education believes that a large number of faculty members and students in elementary, middle, and high schools throughout Guangdong Province still use dialects, which greatly hinders the promotion of national language education compared to other provinces. The Ministry has therefore formulated a five-point outline of measures for promoting national language education in the province, and has telegraphed the Guangdong Provincial Department of Education to develop detailed measures based on this outline and implement them diligently. The original provisions are copied and recorded below: (1) Urge teachers at all levels of schools in the province to teach entirely in the national language. (Inspectors should report on whether teachers at all levels of schools are teaching in the national language, and this should be included in the performance evaluation of each school.) (2) Current Chinese language teachers in normal schools, middle schools, and elementary schools who are unable to teach in the national language should be required by the Department of Education to study within a specified time period. Upon completion, they will be assessed. Those who are able to teach in the national language will be exempt from study and will be directly issued a certificate. (3) Establish national language training centers in important and convenient locations, requiring teachers at all levels of schools who cannot teach in the national language to study in phases. (4) Starting from the 26th academic year, the normal school entrance examination subjects will include national language oral proficiency and phonetic symbols. (5) Starting from the 27th academic year, the examination for elementary school teachers should include national language oral proficiency and phonetic symbols.

Xinmin and 46 Other Schools Requesting Ban on City School Educators' Union Because It Was Not Organized According to Legal Procedures. The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs Publicly Bans It. 208

Recently, Xinmin Elementary School and 46 other municipal schools jointly submitted a request to the Bureau of Social Affairs, stating that a small number of municipal school staff members, including Qian Xuanqing, had organized the Shanghai Municipal School Staff Union without prior notice to Xinmin and the other 46 schools. Furthermore, the union had not been permitted or registered by party and government agencies and did not comply with legal procedures. Therefore, they requested a ban to avoid disputes. After receiving the request, the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs stated that the organization of civic groups must, in accordance with the provisions of Section 3 of the Civic Group Organization Plan, be permitted by local party headquarters at all levels and reported to the government before organizational activities can be carried out. The union had not gone through the aforementioned legal procedures and therefore violated the law. Moreover, the city already had organizations such as the Elementary School Educators' Union, making it unnecessary to establish another organization. A ban was therefore issued and publicly announced.

(Zhenjiang News) The Jiangsu Provincial Council of the Boy Scouts of China convened representatives from various county councils and Boy Scout instructors from county party headquarters in Zhenjiang, Yangzhou, Shanghai, and Xuzhou to hold a joint symposium to discuss the issue of fundraising for the "Jiangsu Boy Scout" aircraft. The first district, including Zhenjiang and 17 other counties, held a meeting in Zhenjiang the day before yesterday to discuss the aircraft fundraising issue. The methods for raising funds for the "Jiangsu Boy Scout" aircraft are recorded below: (1) The total amount of this donation is temporarily set at 100,000 yuan, which will be jointly raised by Boy Scouts and service personnel throughout the province. (2) The amount of this donation to be raised is at least one yuan per elementary school Boy Scout, at least three yuan per middle school Boy Scout, and at least five yuan per service member. (3) This donation must be forwarded by the local council to this association before January 10, 1937. Counties without established councils should send them directly to this association for transfer to the Jiangsu Provincial Aviation Association. (4) The fundraising and management of aircraft donations will be handled by the organizing committee of this association. (5) Every Boy Scout and every service member who raises the specified amount will be given a Class C commemorative badge and a Class C certificate. Those who raise 10 yuan will be given a Class B commemorative badge and a Class B certificate. Those who raise 20 yuan will be given a Class A commemorative badge and a Class A certificate. Those who raise 90 yuan will have a letter sent to Chairman Chen of the Jiangsu Provincial Government requesting special awards. (6) These measures have been decided by the Jiangsu Provincial Council of the Boy Scouts of China and will be implemented. Any matters not covered may be amended by the council from time to time.

Income Tax for Faculty and Staff of Private Schools Falls Under the Scope of Independent Professions; Ministry of Finance Responds to Jiangsu Provincial Government 213

The Jiangsu Provincial Government previously stated that Item 3 of the "Explanation of the Scope of Civil Servants and the Calculation Method of Their Salary Income Tax Amount" stipulated that faculty and staff of national, provincial, municipal, and county schools should fall under the scope of civil servants. However, it was not clearly defined whether faculty and staff of private schools fall under the scope of "other persons engaged in public service according to laws and regulations" or under the scope of independent professions. Therefore, the Provincial Government requested a reply from the Ministry of Finance. The Jiangsu Provincial Government has now received a reply from the Ministry of Finance, which states that the income of faculty and staff of national, provincial, municipal, and county schools is paid from the national or local treasury and should be taxed as civil servants starting in October of this year. However, since the source of income for faculty and staff of private schools is different, they will be taxed as independent professionals starting in January of next year. After receiving the reply, the Jiangsu Provincial Government instructed the Department of Education to comply.

Spring and Autumn

Blue Culture Street 215

Sima Road is known as Shanghai's Culture Street because it is a hub for bookstores. However, a certain Bazhi Road in Hongkou District also carries the same connotation. From Wenhua Book Company at the intersection of North Sichuan Road to North Henan Road, the west part of Bazhi Road is not long. However, there are no less than twenty schools along the road and nearby, including elementary schools and foreign language training schools. Each school has three to four hundred students, or at least dozens, adding up to a considerable number.

When both hands of the clock point upwards, it is time for school to dismiss at noon. Students on the road, male and female, big and small, suddenly crowd the street. Looking from afar, one only sees the swaying of blue, for half an hour. This kind of liveliness cannot be seen on other roads, not even on the university street in Jiangwan.

Perhaps blue is neither too bright nor too dull, aligning with the so-called "doctrine of the mean." Naturally, I love the innocence and vitality of students, their forward momentum, and I also love their blue shirts.

I often stroll along Bazhi Road, especially at noon. Walking through the cultural street of Hongkou District among the students, I cannot help but recite: "Students scatter at noon, blue shirts fill the street."

Lujiawan Bridge 216

— Chen Tianxi

Lujiawan Bridge is located in the middle of Xiexu Road in Nanshi. Five or six years ago, one could still see the wooden bridge. In recent years, the local authorities filled it in, and there is no trace of the bridge anymore. As a result, pedestrians only know of Lujiawan, but not of Lujiawan Bridge.

Before it was filled in, underneath the Lujiawan Bridge was a filthy and smelly mud pool. Every summer, the waste accumulated in the pool over time was exposed to strong sunlight, making people feel dizzy. Therefore, pedestrians regarded it as a path to be avoided.

Originally, the area was very desolate a dozen years ago. Later, the landowners built houses on most of the nearby vacant land, and the number of residents gradually increased, turning it into a bustling working-class area. With so many residents, there was naturally a need to fill in the useless and foul-smelling pool. Therefore, the municipal authorities ordered the Public Works Bureau to find a way to fill it in. The Public Works Bureau used garbage and other waste to accumulate it day by day. It has now been filled in to the west of Lujiawan Bridge. It is expected that soon, even the waste pools at Dapu Bridge, Da Mu Bridge, Fenglin Bridge and other places will be filled in, creating a garbage road.

In the past, transportation in the Lujiawan Bridge area relied on French Route 10 and Route 6 trams. As a result, the China Merchants Tram Company had plans to build a line directly to Xujiawan to prevent external interests from encroaching. However, the waste pool could not be filled in for a while, so it has not yet been realized. Later, the Public Bus Company, sponsored by the Municipal Public Utility Bureau, opened up a route, which began to take away part of the business.

Now that this area has been filled in, it naturally gives those unemployed and poor people a good opportunity until the government authorities announce what it will be used for. At first, there were only people placing manure carts and fortune-tellers setting up stalls to write letters for people. Later, poor people nearby saw that the filled-in area was suitable for setting up stalls, so they contacted the local hooligans and bullies and asked them for protection, with all expenses paid by the poor people on a daily basis. Once this trend started, it was as if people who travel around selling goods came after hearing the news. More and more stalls were set up every day.

From Lujiawan Bridge to Xieqiao, one only sees crowds of people. What comes into view are all stalls. The liveliness is no less than that of the City God Temple. The most numerous are the second-hand stalls, followed by character-breaking stalls, miscellaneous goods stalls, snack stalls, plaster stalls, miscellaneous disease clinics, shoe stalls, martial arts performances, and so on. All kinds of stalls that travel around the world are available.

There was a time when these many stalls were banned by the Municipal Public Security Bureau, but later, somehow, these stalls reappeared in a few days, presumably because someone had lobbied the authorities. In short, although Lujiawan Bridge is now forgotten by people, the poor people who rely on filling in the Lujiawan Bridge to earn a living should commemorate this Lujiawan Bridge.

Yangshupu at Night 217

— Fang Zheng

The god of night stretches out its giant arm, grasping the entire pulse of Yangshupu; the street lights emit a dim light, trams, cars, public buses, rickshaws, small carts, rickshaws, and Japanese military trucks come and go in a constant stream. But for the time being, this is just a flash in the pan!

Although this place is not as luxurious as Nanjing Road, nor as mysterious as Fourth Road, nor as exotic as Avenue Joffre, it also has the same popular touch as Robison Road—the base camp for the working masses and people struggling to make a living—therefore, in the evening, especially at dusk, all the factories here successively release a group of pale-faced and mentally exhausted male and female workers, and at the same time take in a group of thin and haggard men and women working the night shift. For the sake of survival, they do not hesitate to toil all day and take the lowest price.

Maybe it's to find excitement! No! They lack knowledge, so demeaning and teasing of women will come out of their mouths at any time:

"Little sister! Want to go to a room?"

"Elder sister! Want to have some fun?"

But those who are called "little sister" will resist and curse the teasers:

"May you be struck by a thousand knives!" "Pig!"

"Be careful of the tram running you over (to death)!"

Some are in the factory by the foreman's meanness and insults, and in addition to sighing that they have a bad fate, what other way can they think of? Because they need to eat, they have to let people slaughter them, forever slaughter them!

These are daily homework, the only ornaments of Yangshupu every night.

When the short hand of the clock turns to 10 on Albert Road, the whole of Yangshupu is dead, and there is simply no moan. Next to its corpse are only sleepy policemen and the sound of wonton sellers, as well as those who take the risk for survival. (A vicious term for undressing people in the dead of night).

The night in Yangshupu finally disappeared in this way!
